## 三、Agent 系统构建深度解析

### 3.1 Agent 架构模式详解

#### 3.1.1 三种核心架构模式

```
+-------------------------------------------------------------+
|              模式一：ReAct (Reasoning + Acting)             |
+-------------------------------------------------------------+
|                                                             |
|   Thought -> Action -> Observation -> Thought -> ...        |
|                                                             |
|   特点：                                                    |
|   - 交替进行推理和行动                                      |
|   - 每次行动后观察结果，再决定下一步                        |
|   - 适合：需要多步推理、工具调用的场景                      |
|   - 代表：LangChain ReActAgent, AutoGPT                     |
|                                                             |
|   示例流程：                                                 |
|   Thought: 用户想知道北京明天的天气，我需要调用天气 API     |
|   Action: weather_api(city="北京", date="明天")            |
|   Observation: {"temperature": 25, "weather": "晴"}        |
|   Thought: 我已经获取到天气信息，可以回答用户了             |
|   Action: finish(answer="北京明天晴天，25度")              |
|                                                             |
+-------------------------------------------------------------+

+-------------------------------------------------------------+
|              模式二：Plan-and-Execute (规划 + 执行)         |
+-------------------------------------------------------------+
|                                                             |
|   规划阶段                    执行阶段                      |
|   +----------+              +----------+                   |
|   | 分解任务  | -----------> | 逐步执行  |                   |
|   | 生成计划  |              | 监控进度  |                   |
|   +----------+              +----------+                   |
|                                                             |
|   特点：                                                    |
|   - 先制定完整计划，再执行                                  |
|   - 计划可动态调整                                          |
|   - 适合：复杂多步骤任务，需要全局规划                      |
|   - 代表：LangChain PlanAndExecute, BabyAGI                 |
|                                                             |
|   示例：                                                    |
|   Plan: ["搜索公司 Q3 财报", "提取营收和利润数据",           |
|          "与去年同期对比计算增长率", "生成分析报告"]        |
|   Execute: 按步骤执行，每步验证结果后再进入下一步           |
|                                                             |
+-------------------------------------------------------------+

+-------------------------------------------------------------+
|              模式三：Reflexion (自我反思 + 迭代改进)        |
+-------------------------------------------------------------+
|                                                             |
|   尝试 -> 评估 -> 反思 -> 改进 -> 重试 -> ...               |
|                                                             |
|   特点：                                                    |
|   - 引入自我评估和反思机制                                  |
|   - 失败后不终止，而是分析原因并重试                        |
|   - 维护经验教训记忆                                        |
|   - 适合：需要高精度、可自我纠错的长任务                    |
|   - 代表：Reflexion (Shinn et al., 2023)                    |
|                                                             |
+-------------------------------------------------------------+
```

#### 3.1.2 三种模式对比与选择

| 维度 | ReAct | Plan-and-Execute | Reflexion |
|------|-------|------------------|-----------|
| **响应延迟** | 中 | 高 | 高 |
| **任务复杂度** | 中 | 高 | 高 |
| **成功率** | 中 | 中高 | 高 |
| **token 消耗** | 中 | 高 | 很高 |
| **适用场景** | 单轮/多轮工具调用 | 复杂工作流 | 代码生成、精确任务 |
| **实现难度** | 低 | 中 | 高 |
| **可解释性** | 高 | 高 | 很高 |

---

### 3.2 ReAct Agent 完整实现

```python
import json
import asyncio
from typing import List, Dict, Callable, Optional
from dataclasses import dataclass
from enum import Enum

class ActionType(Enum):
    THOUGHT = "thought"
    ACTION = "action"
    OBSERVATION = "observation"
    FINISH = "finish"
    ERROR = "error"

@dataclass
class Tool:
    name: str
    description: str
    parameters: dict
    func: Callable
    
    def to_schema(self) -> dict:
        return {
            "name": self.name,
            "description": self.description,
            "parameters": self.parameters,
        }

@dataclass
class Step:
    step_number: int
    thought: str
    action: Optional[dict] = None
    observation: Optional[str] = None

class ReActAgent:
    """
    完整的 ReAct Agent 实现
    支持多工具调用、异步执行、记忆管理、最大步数限制、错误处理和重试
    """
    
    def __init__(
        self,
        llm_client,
        tools: List[Tool],
        max_steps: int = 15,
        max_retries: int = 3,
        system_prompt: Optional[str] = None,
    ):
        self.llm = llm_client
        self.tools = {tool.name: tool for tool in tools}
        self.max_steps = max_steps
        self.max_retries = max_retries
        self.memory: List[Step] = []
        self.system_prompt = system_prompt or self._default_system_prompt()
    
    def _default_system_prompt(self) -> str:
        tools_desc = "\n".join([
            f"- {name}: {tool.description}"
            for name, tool in self.tools.items()
        ])
        return f"""你是一个智能助手，可以通过思考和调用工具来解决复杂问题。

你可以使用以下工具：
{tools_desc}

请严格按以下格式输出：
Thought: [你的思考过程]
Action: [工具名]([JSON格式的参数])

或者当任务完成时：
Thought: [任务已完成]
Action: finish(answer="[最终答案]")

重要规则：
1. 每次只输出一个 Thought 和一个 Action
2. Action 必须使用有效的 JSON 格式参数
3. 如果工具返回错误，请分析原因并重试或换用其他工具
4. 如果达到最大步数仍未完成，请给出最佳可能的答案
"""
    
    async def run(self, task: str, context: Optional[dict] = None) -> dict:
        step_number = 0
        
        while step_number < self.max_steps:
            step_number += 1
            prompt = self._build_prompt(task, context, step_number)
            
            for retry in range(self.max_retries):
                try:
                    response = await self.llm.generate(
                        prompt, temperature=0.3, max_tokens=500,
                    )
                    break
                except Exception as e:
                    if retry == self.max_retries - 1:
                        return self._error_result(f"LLM 调用失败: {e}")
                    await asyncio.sleep(2 ** retry)
            
            parsed = self._parse_response(response)
            if not parsed:
                self.memory.append(Step(
                    step_number=step_number,
                    thought=f"解析失败: {response}",
                    action={"type": "error", "detail": "parse_failed"},
                ))
                continue
            
            thought = parsed.get("thought", "")
            action = parsed.get("action", {})
            
            if action.get("type") == "finish":
                self.memory.append(Step(
                    step_number=step_number, thought=thought, action=action,
                ))
                return {
                    "success": True,
                    "answer": action.get("answer", ""),
                    "steps": self.memory,
                    "total_steps": step_number,
                }
            
            observation = await self._execute_action(action)
            self.memory.append(Step(
                step_number=step_number,
                thought=thought,
                action=action,
                observation=str(observation)[:1000],
            ))
            
            if observation and isinstance(observation, dict) and observation.get("complete"):
                return {
                    "success": True,
                    "answer": observation.get("result", ""),
                    "steps": self.memory,
                    "total_steps": step_number,
                }
        
        return {
            "success": False,
            "answer": "达到最大步数限制，未能完成任务。",
            "steps": self.memory,
            "total_steps": step_number,
        }
    
    def _build_prompt(self, task: str, context: Optional[dict], step: int) -> str:
        history = "\n\n".join([
            f"Step {s.step_number}:\nThought: {s.thought}\n"
            f"Action: {json.dumps(s.action, ensure_ascii=False) if s.action else 'None'}\n"
            f"Observation: {s.observation or 'None'}"
            for s in self.memory
        ])
        context_str = ""
        if context:
            context_str = f"\n附加上下文：{json.dumps(context, ensure_ascii=False)}\n"
        return f"""{self.system_prompt}

用户任务：{task}{context_str}

执行历史：
{history}

当前是第 {step} 步，请继续：

Thought:"""
    
    def _parse_response(self, response: str) -> Optional[dict]:
        try:
            if "Thought:" in response:
                thought_part = response.split("Thought:")[-1]
                thought = thought_part.split("Action:")[0].strip()
            else:
                thought = response.strip()
            
            if "Action:" in response:
                action_str = response.split("Action:")[-1].strip()
                if action_str.startswith("finish"):
                    answer = action_str.split("(", 1)[1].rsplit(")", 1)[0]
                    try:
                        params = json.loads(answer)
                        return {"thought": thought, "action": {"type": "finish", **params}}
                    except:
                        return {"thought": thought, "action": {"type": "finish", "answer": answer.strip('"')}}
                
                tool_name = action_str.split("(")[0].strip()
                params_str = action_str.split("(", 1)[1].rsplit(")", 1)[0]
                params = json.loads(params_str)
                return {
                    "thought": thought,
                    "action": {"type": "tool_call", "tool": tool_name, "args": params},
                }
            return {"thought": thought, "action": None}
        except Exception:
            return None
    
    async def _execute_action(self, action: dict) -> any:
        if action.get("type") != "tool_call":
            return None
        tool_name = action.get("tool", "")
        args = action.get("args", {})
        if tool_name not in self.tools:
            return {"error": f"未知工具: {tool_name}"}
        tool = self.tools[tool_name]
        try:
            if asyncio.iscoroutinefunction(tool.func):
                return await tool.func(**args)
            return tool.func(**args)
        except Exception as e:
            return {"error": str(e)}
    
    def _error_result(self, error_msg: str) -> dict:
        return {
            "success": False,
            "answer": error_msg,
            "steps": self.memory,
            "total_steps": len(self.memory),
        }


# 工具定义示例
async def search_web(query: str, top_k: int = 5) -> dict:
    return {"results": [f"Result for {query}"], "complete": False}

async def execute_code(code: str, language: str = "python") -> dict:
    return {"output": "", "error": None, "complete": False}

async def query_database(sql: str, database: str = "default") -> dict:
    return {"rows": [], "columns": [], "complete": False}

async def read_file(path: str) -> dict:
    return {"content": "", "complete": False}
```

---

### 3.3 记忆管理系统

#### 3.3.1 三层记忆架构

```
+-------------------------------------------------------------+
|                    记忆层级架构                              |
+-------------------------------------------------------------+
|                                                             |
|  +-------------------------------------------------------+  |
|  | 短期记忆 (Short-term)                                  |  |
|  | - 当前对话上下文                                       |  |
|  | - 最近 N 轮交互                                        |  |
|  | - 存储：内存 / Redis                                   |  |
|  | - 容量：4K-32K tokens                                  |  |
|  | - TTL：会话结束                                        |  |
|  +-------------------------------------------------------+  |
|                          |                                  |
|                          v                                  |
|  +-------------------------------------------------------+  |
|  | 长期记忆 (Long-term)                                   |  |
|  | - 历史对话摘要                                         |  |
|  | - 用户画像和偏好                                       |  |
|  | - 存储：数据库 (PostgreSQL/MongoDB)                    |  |
|  | - 容量：无限制                                         |  |
|  +-------------------------------------------------------+  |
|                          |                                  |
|                          v                                  |
|  +-------------------------------------------------------+  |
|  | 向量记忆 (Vector)                                      |  |
|  | - 语义相似的记忆片段                                   |  |
|  | - 知识片段、事实、实体                                 |  |
|  | - 存储：向量数据库 (Milvus/Qdrant)                     |  |
|  | - 检索：语义相似度                                     |  |
|  +-------------------------------------------------------+  |
|                                                             |
+-------------------------------------------------------------+
```

```python
from typing import List, Optional
from datetime import datetime

class MemoryManager:
    """三层记忆管理：短期记忆 + 长期记忆 + 向量记忆"""
    
    def __init__(self, vector_store, db_client, redis_client):
        self.vector_store = vector_store
        self.db = db_client
        self.redis = redis_client
        self.short_term_limit = 10
    
    async def add_interaction(
        self, session_id: str, role: str, content: str, metadata: Optional[dict] = None,
    ):
        timestamp = datetime.utcnow().isoformat()
        await self._add_to_short_term(session_id, role, content, timestamp)
        await self._add_to_long_term(session_id, role, content, timestamp, metadata)
        await self._add_to_vector_memory(session_id, content, metadata)
    
    async def _add_to_short_term(self, session_id: str, role: str, content: str, timestamp: str):
        key = f"session:{session_id}:history"
        message = json.dumps({"role": role, "content": content, "time": timestamp})
        await self.redis.lpush(key, message)
        await self.redis.ltrim(key, 0, self.short_term_limit * 2 - 1)
        await self.redis.expire(key, 3600 * 24)
    
    async def _add_to_long_term(self, session_id: str, role: str, content: str,
                                 timestamp: str, metadata: Optional[dict]):
        await self.db.execute(
            """INSERT INTO conversation_history
            (session_id, role, content, timestamp, metadata)
            VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5)""",
            session_id, role, content, timestamp, json.dumps(metadata or {}),
        )
    
    async def _add_to_vector_memory(self, session_id: str, content: str, metadata: Optional[dict]):
        embedding = await self._get_embedding(content)
        await self.vector_store.insert(
            vectors=[embedding],
            metadatas=[{
                "session_id": session_id,
                "content": content,
                "timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
                **(metadata or {}),
            }],
        )
    
    async def get_context(
        self, session_id: str, query: str,
        max_short_term: int = 6,
        max_long_term: int = 5,
        max_vector_results: int = 3,
    ) -> dict:
        short_term = await self._get_short_term(session_id, max_short_term)
        long_term = await self._get_long_term(session_id, max_long_term)
        vector_memories = await self._get_vector_memory(session_id, query, max_vector_results)
        return {
            "short_term": short_term,
            "long_term": long_term,
            "vector_memory": vector_memories,
        }
    
    async def _get_short_term(self, session_id: str, limit: int) -> List[dict]:
        key = f"session:{session_id}:history"
        messages = await self.redis.lrange(key, 0, limit - 1)
        return [json.loads(m) for m in messages][::-1]
    
    async def _get_long_term(self, session_id: str, limit: int) -> List[dict]:
        rows = await self.db.fetch(
            """SELECT role, content, timestamp FROM conversation_history
            WHERE session_id = $1 ORDER BY timestamp DESC LIMIT $2""",
            session_id, limit,
        )
        return [{"role": r["role"], "content": r["content"], "time": r["timestamp"]} for r in rows]
    
    async def _get_vector_memory(self, session_id: str, query: str, limit: int) -> List[dict]:
        embedding = await self._get_embedding(query)
        return await self.vector_store.search(
            embedding, top_k=limit, filters={"session_id": session_id},
        )
    
    async def _get_embedding(self, text: str) -> List[float]:
        pass  # 调用 embedding 服务
    
    async def summarize_session(self, session_id: str) -> str:
        history = await self._get_long_term(session_id, limit=1000)
        history_text = "\n".join([f"{h['role']}: {h['content']}" for h in history])
        prompt = f"""请总结以下对话的关键信息：

{history_text}

请提取：1.用户核心需求 2.达成结论 3.用户偏好 4.待跟进事项

摘要（200字以内）："""
        summary = await self.llm.generate(prompt)
        await self._add_to_long_term(
            session_id, "system", f"[会话摘要] {summary}",
            datetime.utcnow().isoformat(), {"type": "summary"},
        )
        return summary
```

---

### 3.4 多 Agent 协作架构

```python
from typing import List
import asyncio

class MultiAgentOrchestrator:
    """
    多 Agent 协作编排器
    支持模式：流水线 / 并行 / 投票 / 路由 / 层级
    """
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.agents: dict[str, ReActAgent] = {}
        self.pipelines: dict[str, List[str]] = {}
    
    def register_agent(self, name: str, agent: ReActAgent):
        self.agents[name] = agent
    
    def define_pipeline(self, name: str, agent_names: List[str]):
        self.pipelines[name] = agent_names
    
    async def run_pipeline(self, pipeline_name: str, input_data: str) -> dict:
        agents = [self.agents[name] for name in self.pipelines[pipeline_name]]
        result = input_data
        outputs = []
        for i, agent in enumerate(agents):
            output = await agent.run(result)
            outputs.append({
                "step": i,
                "agent": self.pipelines[pipeline_name][i],
                "output": output,
            })
            result = output.get("answer", "")
        return {"final_output": result, "intermediate_outputs": outputs}
    
    async def run_parallel(self, agent_names: List[str], input_data: str) -> dict:
        tasks = [self.agents[name].run(input_data) for name in agent_names]
        results = await asyncio.gather(*tasks, return_exceptions=True)
        return {
            "results": [
                {"agent": name, "output": result if not isinstance(result, Exception) else str(result)}
                for name, result in zip(agent_names, results)
            ],
        }
    
    async def run_voting(self, agent_names: List[str], input_data: str) -> dict:
        parallel_result = await self.run_parallel(agent_names, input_data)
        answers = [r["output"].get("answer", "") for r in parallel_result["results"]]
        from collections import Counter
        answer_counts = Counter(answers)
        winner = answer_counts.most_common(1)[0]
        return {
            "winning_answer": winner[0],
            "votes": winner[1],
            "total_agents": len(agent_names),
            "all_answers": answers,
        }
    
    async def run_hierarchical(self, manager_name: str, worker_names: List[str], task: str) -> dict:
        manager = self.agents[manager_name]
        plan_prompt = f"""请分析以下任务，将其分解为子任务。
可用 Worker：{', '.join(worker_names)}

任务：{task}

请按 JSON 输出：[{{"worker": "name", "subtask": "desc"}}]"""
        
        plan_result = await manager.run(plan_prompt)
        try:
            plan = json.loads(plan_result["answer"])
        except:
            plan = [{"worker": worker_names[0], "subtask": task}]
        
        subtask_results = []
        for item in plan:
            worker_name = item.get("worker", worker_names[0])
            subtask = item.get("subtask", "")
            if worker_name in self.agents:
                result = await self.agents[worker_name].run(subtask)
                subtask_results.append({"worker": worker_name, "subtask": subtask, "result": result})
        
        integration_prompt = f"""请整合以下子任务结果，给出最终答案。

原始任务：{task}
子任务结果：{json.dumps(subtask_results, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)}

最终答案："""
        final = await manager.run(integration_prompt)
        return {
            "plan": plan,
            "subtask_results": subtask_results,
            "final_answer": final.get("answer", ""),
        }
```

---

### 3.5 安全沙箱（代码执行隔离）

```python
import tempfile
import os
import docker

class CodeSandbox:
    """
    代码执行沙箱
    安全策略：容器隔离、资源限制、网络隔离、文件系统隔离、非特权运行
    """
    
    def __init__(
        self,
        image: str = "python:3.11-slim",
        timeout: int = 30,
        memory_limit: str = "256m",
        cpu_limit: float = 1.0,
        network_disabled: bool = True,
    ):
        self.image = image
        self.timeout = timeout
        self.memory_limit = memory_limit
        self.cpu_limit = cpu_limit
        self.network_disabled = network_disabled
        self.docker_client = docker.from_env()
    
    async def execute(self, code: str, language: str = "python") -> dict:
        if language == "python":
            return await self._execute_python(code)
        return {"success": False, "error": f"不支持的编程语言: {language}"}
    
    async def _execute_python(self, code: str) -> dict:
        with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(mode='w', suffix='.py', delete=False) as f:
            safe_code = f"""
import sys, resource
resource.setrlimit(resource.RLIMIT_CPU, ({self.timeout}, {self.timeout}))
resource.setrlimit(resource.RLIMIT_AS, (512*1024*1024, 512*1024*1024))
{code}
"""
            f.write(safe_code)
            temp_file = f.name
        
        try:
            container = self.docker_client.containers.run(
                image=self.image,
                command=f"python {os.path.basename(temp_file)}",
                volumes={os.path.dirname(temp_file): {'bind': '/workspace', 'mode': 'ro'}},
                working_dir='/workspace',
                mem_limit=self.memory_limit,
                cpu_period=100000,
                cpu_quota=int(self.cpu_limit * 100000),
                network_disabled=self.network_disabled,
                read_only=True,
                user="nobody",
                security_opt=["no-new-privileges:true"],
                cap_drop=["ALL"],
                detach=True,
            )
            result = container.wait(timeout=self.timeout + 5)
            stdout = container.logs(stdout=True, stderr=False).decode('utf-8')
            stderr = container.logs(stdout=False, stderr=True).decode('utf-8')
            container.remove(force=True)
            return {
                "success": result["StatusCode"] == 0,
                "output": stdout,
                "error": stderr,
            }
        except Exception as e:
            return {"success": False, "output": "", "error": f"沙箱执行错误: {str(e)}"}
        finally:
            try:
                os.unlink(temp_file)
            except:
                pass
```

---

### 3.6 Agent 系统完整 K8s 部署

```yaml
# =============================================
# Agent 系统完整 K8s 部署
# =============================================

---
apiVersion: v1
kind: Namespace
metadata:
  name: agent-system

---
# 1. Agent API 服务
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: agent-api
  namespace: agent-system
spec:
  replicas: 3
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: agent-api
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: agent-api
    spec:
      serviceAccountName: agent-sa
      containers:
        - name: agent
          image: your-agent-api:latest
          ports:
            - containerPort: 8000
          env:
            - name: LLM_BASE_URL
              value: "http://llm-service:8000/v1"
            - name: EMBEDDING_URL
              value: "http://embedding-service:8080"
            - name: VECTOR_DB_URL
              value: "http://milvus-proxy:19530"
            - name: REDIS_URL
              value: "redis://redis:6379/0"
            - name: SANDBOX_URL
              value: "http://sandbox-service:8080"
            - name: MAX_STEPS
              value: "15"
            - name: ENABLE_REFLEXION
              value: "true"
          resources:
            limits:
              memory: "4Gi"
              cpu: "2"
          livenessProbe:
            httpGet:
              path: /health
              port: 8000
            initialDelaySeconds: 30
          readinessProbe:
            httpGet:
              path: /ready
              port: 8000
            initialDelaySeconds: 10
---
apiVersion: v1
kind: Service
metadata:
  name: agent-api
  namespace: agent-system
spec:
  selector:
    app: agent-api
  ports:
    - port: 8000
      targetPort: 8000

---
# 2. 代码执行沙箱服务
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: sandbox-service
  namespace: agent-system
spec:
  replicas: 5
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: sandbox-service
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: sandbox-service
    spec:
      runtimeClassName: gvisor
      containers:
        - name: sandbox
          image: your-sandbox-image:latest
          ports:
            - containerPort: 8080
          env:
            - name: MAX_EXECUTION_TIME
              value: "30"
            - name: MAX_MEMORY
              value: "256m"
            - name: NETWORK_DISABLED
              value: "true"
          resources:
            limits:
              memory: "1Gi"
              cpu: "1"
          securityContext:
            runAsNonRoot: true
            runAsUser: 65534
            readOnlyRootFilesystem: true
            allowPrivilegeEscalation: false
            capabilities:
              drop:
                - ALL
          volumeMounts:
            - name: tmp
              mountPath: /tmp
      volumes:
        - name: tmp
          emptyDir:
            sizeLimit: 500Mi
---
apiVersion: v1
kind: Service
metadata:
  name: sandbox-service
  namespace: agent-system
spec:
  selector:
    app: sandbox-service
  ports:
    - port: 8080
      targetPort: 8080

---
# 3. Agent Worker（异步任务处理）
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: agent-worker
  namespace: agent-system
spec:
  replicas: 3
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: agent-worker
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: agent-worker
    spec:
      containers:
        - name: worker
          image: your-agent-worker:latest
          env:
            - name: REDIS_URL
              value: "redis://redis:6379/1"
            - name: LLM_BASE_URL
              value: "http://llm-service:8000/v1"
            - name: CONCURRENCY
              value: "5"
          resources:
            limits:
              memory: "2Gi"
              cpu: "2"
```

---

## 四、模型微调与持续学习

### 4.1 微调策略深度对比

#### 4.1.1 全参数微调 vs 参数高效微调

| 维度 | 全参数微调 (Full Fine-tuning) | LoRA | QLoRA | DoRA | Prompt Tuning |
|------|------------------------------|------|-------|------|---------------|
| **可训练参数量** | 100% | 0.1-1% | 0.1-1% | 0.1-1% | <0.01% |
| **显存需求 (7B)** | 56-112GB | 16-20GB | 8-12GB | 16-20GB | 14-16GB |
| **显存需求 (13B)** | 104-208GB | 24-28GB | 12-16GB | 24-28GB | 22-24GB |
| **训练速度** | 慢 | 快 | 较快 | 快 | 最快 |
| **效果** | 最佳 | 很好 | 好 | 很好+ | 一般 |
| **多任务切换** | 需多个模型 | 切换 adapter | 切换 adapter | 切换 adapter | 切换 soft prompt |
| **实现难度** | 低 | 低 | 中 | 中 | 低 |
| **适用场景** | 数据充足、追求极致 | 推荐默认 | 消费级显卡 | 高精度需求 | 快速实验 |

#### 4.1.2 LoRA / QLoRA / DoRA / Prompt Tuning 详解

**LoRA (Low-Rank Adaptation)**：

```
原理：冻结预训练权重 W0，训练低秩矩阵 A 和 B
      W = W0 + BA
      其中 B (d x r), A (r x k), r << min(d, k)

优点：
- 参数量极少（通常 <1%）
- 不引入推理延迟（可合并到基础模型）
- 多个任务可切换不同 adapter

超参数：
- rank (r): 8-256，常用 64
- alpha: 2*r，常用 128
- target_modules: 注意力层 (q_proj, k_proj, v_proj, o_proj)
- dropout: 0.05-0.1
```

**QLoRA (Quantized LoRA)**：

```
原理：基础模型 4-bit 量化 + LoRA 微调
      使用 NF4 (Normal Float 4) 量化 + 双量化

关键组件：
- 4-bit NormalFloat (NF4)
- Double Quantization (量化常数也量化)
- Paged Optimizers (CPU 分页优化器)

优点：
- 单卡 24GB 可微调 65B 模型
- 效果接近全量微调

注意事项：
- 需要使用 bfloat16 计算
- 数据集质量要求更高
```

**DoRA (Weight-Decomposed Low-Rank Adaptation)**：

```
原理：将权重分解为幅度 (magnitude) 和方向 (direction)
      W = m * (W0/||W0|| + BA/||BA||)
      训练 m（幅度向量）和 BA（方向低秩矩阵）

优点：
- 比 LoRA 更稳定
- 微调效果更接近全参数微调
- 尤其擅长数学和代码任务

缺点：
- 参数量比 LoRA 略多
- 训练时间略长
```

**Prompt Tuning / Prefix Tuning**：

```
Prompt Tuning：
  原理：在输入前添加可训练的 soft prompt tokens (virtual tokens)
  参数量：极少，通常只有几千到几万参数
  适用：快速实验、轻量适配

Prefix Tuning：
  原理：在每一层的 key 和 value 前添加可训练前缀
  参数量：比 Prompt Tuning 多，但比 LoRA 少
  适用：需要更深层表示的任务
```

---

### 4.2 数据集准备与清洗

#### 4.2.1 数据格式规范

```python
# 标准指令微调格式 (Alpaca / ShareGPT)
[
    {
        "instruction": "请总结以下文本",
        "input": "文本内容...",
        "output": "摘要内容...",
        "system": "你是一个专业的文本摘要助手",  # 可选
    },
    {
        "conversations": [
            {"from": "human", "value": "用户问题"},
            {"from": "gpt", "value": "助手回答"},
            {"from": "human", "value": "追问"},
            {"from": "gpt", "value": "回答"},
        ]
    }
]

# 对话格式 (ChatML)
[
    {
        "messages": [
            {"role": "system", "content": "系统提示"},
            {"role": "user", "content": "用户输入"},
            {"role": "assistant", "content": "助手回答"},
        ]
    }
]
```

#### 4.2.2 数据清洗流水线

```python
import re
from typing import List, Dict

class DataCleaner:
    """数据清洗流水线"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.min_length = 10
        self.max_length = 4096
    
    def clean(self, samples: List[Dict]) -> List[Dict]:
        """完整清洗流程"""
        cleaned = samples
        cleaned = self._remove_duplicates(cleaned)
        cleaned = self._filter_length(cleaned)
        cleaned = self._remove_pii(cleaned)
        cleaned = self._fix_format(cleaned)
        cleaned = self._quality_score(cleaned)
        cleaned = self._filter_low_quality(cleaned)
        return cleaned
    
    def _remove_duplicates(self, samples: List[Dict]) -> List[Dict]:
        """去重（基于文本相似度）"""
        seen = set()
        unique = []
        for s in samples:
            key = self._hash_sample(s)
            if key not in seen:
                seen.add(key)
                unique.append(s)
        return unique
    
    def _hash_sample(self, sample: Dict) -> str:
        """生成样本指纹"""
        text = sample.get("instruction", "") + sample.get("input", "") + sample.get("output", "")
        # 简化后取前50字符的 hash
        return hash(text[:200]) & 0xFFFFFFFF
    
    def _filter_length(self, samples: List[Dict]) -> List[Dict]:
        """过滤过长/过短样本"""
        filtered = []
        for s in samples:
            total_len = len(s.get("instruction", "")) + len(s.get("input", "")) + len(s.get("output", ""))
            if self.min_length <= total_len <= self.max_length:
                filtered.append(s)
        return filtered
    
    def _remove_pii(self, samples: List[Dict]) -> List[Dict]:
        """移除 PII 信息"""
        pii_patterns = [
            (r'\b1[3-9]\d{9}\b', '[PHONE]'),  # 手机号
            (r'\b[A-Za-z0-9._%+-]+@[A-Za-z0-9.-]+\.[A-Z|a-z]{2,}\b', '[EMAIL]'),  # 邮箱
            (r'\b\d{17}[\dXx]\b', '[ID]'),  # 身份证号
            (r'\b\d{16}\b', '[CARD]'),  # 银行卡号
        ]
        
        cleaned = []
        for s in samples:
            for key in ["instruction", "input", "output"]:
                if key in s:
                    for pattern, replacement in pii_patterns:
                        s[key] = re.sub(pattern, replacement, s[key])
            cleaned.append(s)
        return cleaned
    
    def _fix_format(self, samples: List[Dict]) -> List[Dict]:
        """修复格式问题"""
        fixed = []
        for s in samples:
            # 移除控制字符
            for key in ["instruction", "input", "output"]:
                if key in s:
                    s[key] = re.sub(r'[\x00-\x08\x0b\x0c\x0e-\x1f]', '', s[key])
                    s[key] = s[key].strip()
            fixed.append(s)
        return fixed
    
    def _quality_score(self, samples: List[Dict]) -> List[Dict]:
        """计算数据质量分"""
        for s in samples:
            score = 0
            output = s.get("output", "")
            
            # 长度合理性
            if 50 <= len(output) <= 2000:
                score += 20
            
            # 包含中文（中文场景）
            if re.search(r'[\u4e00-\u9fff]', output):
                score += 20
            
            # 句子完整性
            if output.endswith(("。", "！", "？", ".", "!", "?", "\"")):
                score += 15
            
            # 无乱码
            if not re.search(r'[^\w\s\u4e00-\u9fff\u3000-\u303f\uff00-\uffef.,;:!?()\[\]{}"\'-]', output):
                score += 15
            
            # 无重复内容（简单检测）
            words = output.split()
            if len(words) > 0 and len(set(words)) / len(words) > 0.5:
                score += 15
            
            # 有实质内容（非纯占位符）
            if len(output) > 20 and not output.startswith(("TODO", "待补充", "...")):
                score += 15
            
            s["quality_score"] = score
        return samples
    
    def _filter_low_quality(self, samples: List[Dict], threshold: int = 60) -> List[Dict]:
        """过滤低质量数据"""
        return [s for s in samples if s.get("quality_score", 0) >= threshold]


class DataAugmenter:
    """数据增强技术"""
    
    def __init__(self, llm_client):
        self.llm = llm_client
    
    async def paraphrase(self, sample: Dict, num_variants: int = 3) -> List[Dict]:
        """同义改写增强"""
        variants = []
        for _ in range(num_variants):
            prompt = f"""请改写以下指令，保持语义不变但表达方式不同：

原指令：{sample['instruction']}

改写："""
            new_instruction = await self.llm.generate(prompt, max_tokens=200)
            variants.append({
                **sample,
                "instruction": new_instruction.strip(),
                "augmented": True,
            })
        return variants
    
    async def back_translation(self, sample: Dict) -> Dict:
        """回译增强：中文 -> 英文 -> 中文"""
        # 先翻译为英文
        prompt1 = f"将以下中文翻译为英文：{sample['output']}"
        english = await self.llm.generate(prompt1, max_tokens=500)
        
        # 再翻译回中文
        prompt2 = f"将以下英文翻译为中文：{english}"
        chinese = await self.llm.generate(prompt2, max_tokens=500)
        
        return {
            **sample,
            "output": chinese.strip(),
            "augmented": True,
        }
    
    def format_diversity(self, sample: Dict) -> List[Dict]:
        """格式多样性增强"""
        variants = []
        
        # 变体1：添加角色设定
        variants.append({
            **sample,
            "system": "你是一位领域专家，请专业地回答。",
        })
        
        # 变体2：改变语气
        variants.append({
            **sample,
            "instruction": sample["instruction"] + "（请用简洁的语言回答）",
        })
        
        # 变体3：添加约束
        variants.append({
            **sample,
            "instruction": sample["instruction"] + "（请分步骤说明）",
        })
        
        return variants
```

---

### 4.3 训练超参数调优

| 超参数 | 建议范围 | 默认值 | 说明 |
|--------|----------|--------|------|
| **learning_rate** | 1e-5 ~ 5e-4 | 2e-4 (LoRA) | 学习率过大导致灾难性遗忘 |
| **batch_size** | 1 ~ 16 | 4 | 受显存限制，可用梯度累积 |
| **gradient_accumulation** | 1 ~ 32 | 4 | 等效 batch_size = batch * accumulation |
| **num_epochs** | 1 ~ 10 | 3 | 通常 3 个 epoch 足够 |
| **warmup_ratio** | 0.01 ~ 0.1 | 0.03 | 预热步数，稳定训练初期 |
| **lr_scheduler** | cosine / linear / constant | cosine | cosine 通常效果最好 |
| **weight_decay** | 0 ~ 0.1 | 0.01 | 防止过拟合 |
| **max_length** | 512 ~ 8192 | 2048 | 根据任务调整 |
| **lora_r** | 8 ~ 256 | 64 | rank 越高表达能力越强 |
| **lora_alpha** | 2*r ~ 4*r | 128 | 缩放因子 |
| **lora_dropout** | 0 ~ 0.1 | 0.05 | 防止过拟合 |
| **max_grad_norm** | 0.3 ~ 1.0 | 0.3 | 梯度裁剪 |

---

### 4.4 评估方法详解

```python
class ModelEvaluator:
    """模型评估框架"""
    
    def __init__(self, model, tokenizer):
        self.model = model
        self.tokenizer = tokenizer
    
    def evaluate_generation(self, test_data: list) -> dict:
        """生成任务评估：BLEU / ROUGE / BERTScore"""
        from rouge import Rouge
        from bert_score import score as bert_score
        
        predictions = []
        references = []
        
        for item in test_data:
            pred = self.generate(item["input"])
            predictions.append(pred)
            references.append(item["output"])
        
        # ROUGE
        rouge = Rouge()
        rouge_scores = rouge.get_scores(predictions, references, avg=True)
        
        # BERTScore
        P, R, F1 = bert_score(predictions, references, lang="zh")
        
        return {
            "rouge-1": rouge_scores["rouge-1"]["f"],
            "rouge-2": rouge_scores["rouge-2"]["f"],
            "rouge-l": rouge_scores["rouge-l"]["f"],
            "bertscore_precision": P.mean().item(),
            "bertscore_recall": R.mean().item(),
            "bertscore_f1": F1.mean().item(),
        }
    
    def evaluate_code(self, test_data: list) -> dict:
        """代码任务评估：HumanEval / MBPP"""
        passed = 0
        total = len(test_data)
        
        for item in test_data:
            code = self.generate(item["prompt"])
            if self._run_tests(code, item["test_cases"]):
                passed += 1
        
        return {
            "pass_at_1": passed / total,
            "total": total,
            "passed": passed,
        }
    
    def _run_tests(self, code: str, test_cases: list) -> bool:
        """执行测试用例"""
        try:
            exec(code)
            for test in test_cases:
                exec(test)
            return True
        except:
            return False
    
    def evaluate_classification(self, test_data: list) -> dict:
        """分类任务评估：Accuracy / F1"""
        from sklearn.metrics import accuracy_score, f1_score, classification_report
        
        predictions = []
        labels = []
        
        for item in test_data:
            pred = self.generate(item["input"])
            predictions.append(pred.strip())
            labels.append(item["label"])
        
        return {
            "accuracy": accuracy_score(labels, predictions),
            "f1_macro": f1_score(labels, predictions, average="macro"),
            "f1_weighted": f1_score(labels, predictions, average="weighted"),
        }
```

---

### 4.5 完整的 K8s Training Job

```yaml
apiVersion: batch/v1
kind: Job
metadata:
  name: lora-finetune-qwen
  namespace: training
spec:
  backoffLimit: 2
  ttlSecondsAfterFinished: 86400
  template:
    spec:
      nodeSelector:
        nvidia.com/gpu.product: NVIDIA-A100-SXM4-80GB
      tolerations:
        - key: nvidia.com/gpu
          operator: Exists
          effect: NoSchedule
      containers:
        - name: trainer
          image: pytorch/pytorch:2.3.0-cuda12.1-cudnn8-runtime
          command:
            - python
            - train.py
          args:
            - --model_name=Qwen/Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct
            - --dataset=/data/business_data.jsonl
            - --output_dir=/models/lora-adapter
            - --lora_r=64
            - --lora_alpha=128
            - --lora_dropout=0.05
            - --target_modules=q_proj,k_proj,v_proj,o_proj,gate_proj,up_proj,down_proj
            - --batch_size=4
            - --gradient_accumulation_steps=4
            - --num_epochs=3
            - --learning_rate=2e-4
            - --max_length=2048
            - --warmup_ratio=0.03
            - --lr_scheduler_type=cosine
            - --bf16=true
            - --save_steps=500
            - --eval_steps=250
            - --logging_steps=10
            - --deepspeed=/config/ds_config_zero2.json
          resources:
            limits:
              nvidia.com/gpu: 4
              memory: "256Gi"
              cpu: "32"
            requests:
              nvidia.com/gpu: 4
              memory: "128Gi"
              cpu: "16"
          volumeMounts:
            - name: data
              mountPath: /data
            - name: model-output
              mountPath: /models
            - name: config
              mountPath: /config
            - name: dshm
              mountPath: /dev/shm
      volumes:
        - name: data
          persistentVolumeClaim:
            claimName: training-data-pvc
        - name: model-output
          persistentVolumeClaim:
            claimName: model-output-pvc
        - name: config
          configMap:
            name: training-config
        - name: dshm
          emptyDir:
            medium: Memory
            sizeLimit: 32Gi
      restartPolicy: Never
```

### 4.6 持续学习流水线（Argo Workflow）

```yaml
apiVersion: argoproj.io/v1alpha1
kind: Workflow
metadata:
  name: continuous-learning-pipeline
  namespace: training
spec:
  entrypoint: pipeline
  templates:
    - name: pipeline
      steps:
        - - name: collect-feedback
            template: collect-feedback
        - - name: auto-label
            template: auto-label
        - - name: data-validation
            template: data-validation
        - - name: train-lora
            template: train-lora
        - - name: evaluate
            template: evaluate
        - - name: compare-with-production
            template: compare-models
        - - name: canary-deploy
            template: canary-deploy
            when: "{{steps.compare-with-production.outputs.parameters.better}} == true"
        - - name: full-deploy
            template: full-deploy
            when: "{{steps.canary-deploy.outputs.parameters.canary-pass}} == true"
    
    - name: collect-feedback
      container:
        image: data-collector:latest
        env:
          - name: DB_URL
            valueFrom:
              secretKeyRef:
                name: db-secret
                key: url
        command: [python, collect.py]
        args:
          - --output=/data/feedback.jsonl
          - --days=7
      outputs:
        artifacts:
          - name: feedback-data
            path: /data/feedback.jsonl
    
    - name: auto-label
      container:
        image: label-studio-ml:latest
        command: [python, auto_label.py]
        args:
          - --input=/data/feedback.jsonl
          - --output=/data/labeled.jsonl
          - --model=gpt-4o
      inputs:
        artifacts:
          - name: feedback-data
            path: /data/feedback.jsonl
      outputs:
        artifacts:
          - name: labeled-data
            path: /data/labeled.jsonl
    
    - name: data-validation
      container:
        image: data-validation:latest
        command: [python, validate.py]
        args:
          - --input=/data/labeled.jsonl
          - --min-samples=100
          - --quality-threshold=70
      inputs:
        artifacts:
          - name: labeled-data
            path: /data/labeled.jsonl
    
    - name: train-lora
      container:
        image: pytorch-training:latest
        resources:
          limits:
            nvidia.com/gpu: 4
            memory: 256Gi
        command: [python, train.py]
        args:
          - --dataset=/data/labeled.jsonl
          - --output=/models/new-adapter
          - --epochs=3
          - --lora_r=64
          - --batch_size=4
      inputs:
        artifacts:
          - name: labeled-data
            path: /data/labeled.jsonl
      outputs:
        artifacts:
          - name: model-output
            path: /models/new-adapter
    
    - name: evaluate
      container:
        image: eval-framework:latest
        command: [python, evaluate.py]
        args:
          - --model=/models/new-adapter
          - --test-set=/data/test-set.jsonl
          - --output=/results/eval.json
      inputs:
        artifacts:
          - name: model-output
            path: /models/new-adapter
      outputs:
        artifacts:
          - name: eval-results
            path: /results/eval.json
        parameters:
          - name: accuracy
            valueFrom:
              path: /results/eval.json
              jsonPath: $.accuracy
    
    - name: compare-models
      container:
        image: eval-framework:latest
        command: [python, compare.py]
        args:
          - --new-results=/results/eval.json
          - --baseline-results=/results/baseline.json
          - --output=/results/compare.json
      inputs:
        artifacts:
          - name: eval-results
            path: /results/eval.json
      outputs:
        parameters:
          - name: better
            valueFrom:
              path: /results/compare.json
              jsonPath: $.is_better
    
    - name: canary-deploy
      container:
        image: kubectl:latest
        command: [bash, -c]
        args:
          - |
            kubectl set image deployment/llm-service \
              vllm=your-registry/llm:new-adapter -n production
            kubectl patch deployment llm-service -n production \
              -p '{"spec":{"strategy":{"type":"RollingUpdate","rollingUpdate":{"maxSurge":1,"maxUnavailable":0}}}}'
            sleep 300
            # 检查金丝雀指标
            python check_canary.py --threshold=0.9
      outputs:
        parameters:
          - name: canary-pass
            valueFrom:
              path: /tmp/canary-result.txt
    
    - name: full-deploy
      container:
        image: kubectl:latest
        command: [bash, -c]
        args:
          - |
            kubectl rollout status deployment/llm-service -n production
            kubectl annotate deployment llm-service -n production \
              model-version=$(date +%Y%m%d-%H%M%S)
```

## 五、业务落地与效果评估

### 5.1 行业案例深度分析

#### 5.1.1 金融行业：智能投研助手

**业务场景**：证券公司研究员每日需要阅读数百份研报、财报、新闻，提取关键信息并生成投资观点。

**技术方案**：

```
+-------------------------------------------------------------+
|                    金融投研助手架构                          |
+-------------------------------------------------------------+
|                                                             |
|  数据源                                                     |
|  +----------+  +----------+  +----------+  +----------+    |
|  | 研报 PDF |  | 财报数据 |  | 新闻 API |  | 公告 OCR |    |
|  +----------+  +----------+  +----------+  +----------+    |
|       |             |             |             |           |
|       v             v             v             v           |
|  +-----------------------------------------------------+   |
|  |              数据管道 (实时/批量摄入)                  |   |
|  |  解析 -> 提取 -> 结构化 -> Embedding -> 向量存储      |   |
|  +-----------------------------------------------------+   |
|       |                                                     |
|       v                                                     |
|  +-----------------------------------------------------+   |
|  |                     RAG 系统                           |   |
|  |  多路检索：研报 + 财报 + 新闻 + 法规                   |   |
|  |  重排序：bge-reranker + 时间衰减                       |   |
|  +-----------------------------------------------------+   |
|       |                                                     |
|       v                                                     |
|  +-----------------------------------------------------+   |
|  |                     Agent 系统                         |   |
|  |  研报摘要 Agent -> 数据对比 Agent -> 观点生成 Agent    |   |
|  |  工具：SQL 查询 / 图表生成 / 数据计算                  |   |
|  +-----------------------------------------------------+   |
|       |                                                     |
|       v                                                     |
|  +-----------------------------------------------------+   |
|  |                     输出层                             |   |
|  |  投资观点 / 风险提示 / 对比图表 / 数据来源引用         |   |
|  +-----------------------------------------------------+   |
|                                                             |
+-------------------------------------------------------------+
```

**关键指标**：
- 研报阅读时间：从 2 小时/份 -> 5 分钟/份
- 信息覆盖率：从 60% -> 95%
- 观点一致性：人工 vs AI 一致性 85%
- 幻觉率：< 3%（严格引用来源）

#### 5.1.2 医疗行业：病历智能分析

**业务场景**：三甲医院每日产生数千份病历，需要自动提取关键信息、生成摘要、辅助编码。

**技术方案**：
- 领域微调：使用医疗领域数据对 7B 模型进行 LoRA 微调
- 多模态：支持文本 + 影像报告 + 检验单
- 合规：本地化部署，数据不出院
- 安全：幻觉检测 + 医生确认机制

**关键指标**：
- ICD 编码准确率：92%
- 病历摘要时间：从 30 分钟 -> 2 分钟
- 医生采纳率：78%
- 数据安全：100% 院内处理

#### 5.1.3 法律行业：合同智能审查

**业务方案**：
- 知识库：法律法规库 + 历史合同库 + 判例库
- 分块策略：按条款级别分块（语义分块）
- 审查 Agent：风险识别 -> 条款对比 -> 修改建议
- 输出：风险报告 + 修改建议 + 法律依据引用

**关键指标**：
- 审查时间：从 4 小时 -> 30 分钟
- 风险发现率：从 75% -> 95%
- 律师采纳建议率：85%
- 漏检率：< 5%

#### 5.1.4 教育行业：个性化智能辅导

**业务方案**：
- 学生画像：知识掌握度 + 学习偏好 + 错题分析
- RAG：教材 + 讲义 + 历年真题 + 知识点库
- Agent：诊断 -> 讲解 -> 练习 -> 评估
- 记忆：长期跟踪学生知识图谱

**关键指标**：
- 答疑覆盖率：95%
- 学生满意度：4.5/5
- 成绩提升率：平均 15%
- 教师工作量减少：30%

#### 5.1.5 制造行业：设备故障诊断

**业务方案**：
- 多模态：设备日志 + 传感器数据 + 维修手册
- RAG：设备手册 + 故障案例库 + 维修记录
- Agent：故障分析 -> 根因定位 -> 维修方案 -> 备件推荐
- 边缘部署：工厂内网本地化推理

**关键指标**：
- MTTR（平均修复时间）降低 60%
- 故障诊断准确率：88%
- 备件预测准确率：82%
- 产线停机时间减少：45%

### 5.2 A/B 测试框架设计

```python
class ABTestFramework:
    """A/B 测试框架"""
    
    def __init__(self, traffic_split: float = 0.2):
        self.traffic_split = traffic_split
    
    def assign_variant(self, user_id: str) -> str:
        """根据用户 ID 分配实验组"""
        import hashlib
        hash_val = int(hashlib.md5(user_id.encode()).hexdigest(), 16)
        if hash_val % 100 < int(self.traffic_split * 100):
            return "treatment"  # 实验组（新模型）
        return "control"  # 对照组（旧模型）
    
    def evaluate(self, control_metrics: dict, treatment_metrics: dict) -> dict:
        """统计显著性检验"""
        from scipy import stats
        
        # T 检验
        t_stat, p_value = stats.ttest_ind(
            treatment_metrics["values"],
            control_metrics["values"],
        )
        
        # 计算提升率
        control_mean = sum(control_metrics["values"]) / len(control_metrics["values"])
        treatment_mean = sum(treatment_metrics["values"]) / len(treatment_metrics["values"])
        lift = (treatment_mean - control_mean) / control_mean * 100
        
        return {
            "control_mean": control_mean,
            "treatment_mean": treatment_mean,
            "lift_percent": lift,
            "p_value": p_value,
            "significant": p_value < 0.05,
            "recommendation": "promote" if p_value < 0.05 and lift > 0 else "keep",
        }
```

```yaml
# KServe A/B 测试
apiVersion: serving.kserve.io/v1beta1
kind: InferenceService
metadata:
  name: llm-ab-test
  namespace: production
spec:
  predictor:
    canaryTrafficPercent: 20
    model:
      modelFormat:
        name: custom
      storageUri: s3://models/v2
      runtime: kserve-llm
  transformer:
    containers:
      - name: ab-test-router
        image: ab-test-router:latest
        env:
          - name: MODEL_A_URL
            value: "http://llm-v1:8000"
          - name: MODEL_B_URL
            value: "http://llm-v2:8000"
          - name: TRAFFIC_SPLIT
            value: "0.2"
```

### 5.3 效果评估指标体系

```python
class ComprehensiveEvaluator:
    """综合效果评估"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.metrics = {}
    
    def evaluate_all(self, test_set: list) -> dict:
        return {
            "retrieval": self._evaluate_retrieval(test_set),
            "generation": self._evaluate_generation(test_set),
            "rag": self._evaluate_rag(test_set),
            "agent": self._evaluate_agent(test_set),
            "business": self._evaluate_business(test_set),
        }
    
    def _evaluate_retrieval(self, test_set: list) -> dict:
        """检索评估"""
        recalls = []
        precisions = []
        
        for item in test_set:
            retrieved = self.rag.retrieve(item["question"])
            retrieved_ids = {doc["id"] for doc in retrieved}
            relevant_ids = set(item["relevant_doc_ids"])
            
            tp = len(retrieved_ids & relevant_ids)
            recalls.append(tp / len(relevant_ids) if relevant_ids else 0)
            precisions.append(tp / len(retrieved_ids) if retrieved_ids else 0)
        
        return {
            "recall@k": sum(recalls) / len(recalls),
            "precision@k": sum(precisions) / len(precisions),
            "f1@k": 2 * sum(precisions) * sum(recalls) / (sum(precisions) + sum(recalls)),
        }
    
    def _evaluate_generation(self, test_set: list) -> dict:
        """生成评估"""
        bleu_scores = []
        rouge_scores = []
        
        for item in test_set:
            answer = self.rag.generate(item["question"])
            # BLEU
            bleu = self._calculate_bleu(answer, item["expected_answer"])
            bleu_scores.append(bleu)
            # ROUGE
            rouge = self._calculate_rouge(answer, item["expected_answer"])
            rouge_scores.append(rouge)
        
        return {
            "bleu": sum(bleu_scores) / len(bleu_scores),
            "rouge_l": sum(rouge_scores) / len(rouge_scores),
        }
    
    def _evaluate_rag(self, test_set: list) -> dict:
        """RAG 端到端评估"""
        hallucination_rates = []
        citation_rates = []
        
        for item in test_set:
            answer = self.rag.generate(item["question"])
            # 幻觉检测
            hallucination = self._detect_hallucination(answer, item.get("ground_truth", ""))
            hallucination_rates.append(hallucination)
            # 引用率
            has_citation = "[" in answer and "]" in answer
            citation_rates.append(1 if has_citation else 0)
        
        return {
            "hallucination_rate": sum(hallucination_rates) / len(hallucination_rates),
            "citation_rate": sum(citation_rates) / len(citation_rates),
            "answer_accuracy": self._llm_judge_batch(test_set),
        }
    
    def _evaluate_agent(self, test_set: list) -> dict:
        """Agent 评估"""
        success_rates = []
        avg_steps = []
        
        for item in test_set:
            result = self.agent.run(item["task"])
            success_rates.append(1 if result["success"] else 0)
            avg_steps.append(result["total_steps"])
        
        return {
            "success_rate": sum(success_rates) / len(success_rates),
            "avg_steps": sum(avg_steps) / len(avg_steps),
        }
    
    def _evaluate_business(self, test_set: list) -> dict:
        """业务指标评估"""
        # 用户满意度、任务完成率、响应时间
        return {
            "user_satisfaction": self._survey_nps(),
            "task_completion_rate": self._track_completion(),
            "avg_response_time": self._track_latency(),
            "cost_per_query": self._track_cost(),
        }
```

### 5.4 用户反馈闭环

```python
class FeedbackLoop:
    """用户反馈闭环系统"""
    
    def __init__(self, db, vector_store):
        self.db = db
        self.vector_store = vector_store
    
    async def collect_feedback(self, query_id: str, feedback: dict):
        """收集用户反馈"""
        await self.db.execute(
            """INSERT INTO feedback
            (query_id, rating, comment, thumbs_up, correct_answer, timestamp)
            VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, NOW())""",
            query_id,
            feedback.get("rating"),
            feedback.get("comment"),
            feedback.get("thumbs_up"),
            feedback.get("correct_answer"),
        )
        
        # 如果用户提供了正确答案，加入训练数据池
        if feedback.get("correct_answer"):
            await self._add_to_training_pool(query_id, feedback["correct_answer"])
    
    async def _add_to_training_pool(self, query_id: str, correct_answer: str):
        """加入训练数据池"""
        # 获取原始查询
        query = await self.db.fetchval(
            "SELECT query FROM queries WHERE id = $1", query_id,
        )
        
        # 加入待标注队列
        await self.db.execute(
            """INSERT INTO training_pool
            (query, expected_answer, source, status, created_at)
            VALUES ($1, $2, 'user_feedback', 'pending', NOW())""",
            query, correct_answer,
        )
    
    async def trigger_retrain(self, threshold: int = 100):
        """触发重新训练"""
        # 检查待训练数据量
        count = await self.db.fetchval(
            "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM training_pool WHERE status = 'pending'",
        )
        
        if count >= threshold:
            # 触发 Argo Workflow
            import subprocess
            subprocess.run([
                "argo", "submit", 
                "--watch",
                "/workflows/continuous-learning.yaml",
            ])
            
            # 标记为已使用
            await self.db.execute(
                "UPDATE training_pool SET status = 'used' WHERE status = 'pending'",
            )
    
    async def weekly_report(self) -> dict:
        """生成周度反馈报告"""
        return await self.db.fetch(
            """SELECT
                COUNT(*) as total_feedback,
                AVG(rating) as avg_rating,
                SUM(CASE WHEN thumbs_up THEN 1 ELSE 0 END)::float / COUNT(*) as thumbs_up_rate,
                COUNT(CASE WHEN correct_answer IS NOT NULL THEN 1 END) as corrections
            FROM feedback
            WHERE timestamp > NOW() - INTERVAL '7 days'""",
        )
```

## 六、成本控制策略

### 6.1 分层模型策略（模型路由）

```
用户请求
   |
   v
+-------------------------------------------------------------+
|                    意图识别层 (Tiny Model)                   |
|              Qwen-1.8B / Phi-3-mini / Gemma-2B              |
|                   成本：大模型的 1/100                       |
+-------------------------------------------------------------+
   |
   v
+----------+----------+----------+----------+----------+
|          |          |          |          |          |
简单查询   中等任务   复杂推理   创意生成   代码任务
   |          |          |          |          |
   v          v          v          v          v
+------+  +------+  +------+  +------+  +------+
| 7B   |  | 13B  |  | 33B  |  | 72B  |  | 72B  |
| $0.5 |  | $1.0 |  | $2.0 |  | $3.0 |  | $3.0 |
+------+  +------+  +------+  +------+  +------+
```

```python
class SmartRouter:
    """智能模型路由"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.models = {
            "tiny": {"model": "Qwen/Qwen2.5-1.8B", "cost_per_1m": 0.1},
            "small": {"model": "Qwen/Qwen2.5-7B", "cost_per_1m": 0.5},
            "medium": {"model": "Qwen/Qwen2.5-14B", "cost_per_1m": 1.0},
            "large": {"model": "Qwen/Qwen2.5-72B", "cost_per_1m": 3.0},
        }
        self.classifier = self._load_classifier()
    
    def _load_classifier(self):
        # 加载意图分类模型
        pass
    
    async def route(self, query: str) -> dict:
        # 1. 意图复杂度评分
        complexity = await self._classify_complexity(query)
        
        # 2. 选择模型
        if complexity < 0.2:
            selected = "tiny"
        elif complexity < 0.4:
            selected = "small"
        elif complexity < 0.7:
            selected = "medium"
        else:
            selected = "large"
        
        # 3. 小模型结果置信度低时 fallback
        result = await self._call_model(selected, query)
        if result["confidence"] < 0.8 and selected != "large":
            result = await self._call_model("large", query)
            selected = "large"
        
        return {
            "model": self.models[selected]["model"],
            "complexity": complexity,
            "confidence": result["confidence"],
            "cost": self.models[selected]["cost_per_1m"] * result["tokens"] / 1e6,
        }
    
    async def _classify_complexity(self, query: str) -> float:
        """返回 0-1 的复杂度评分"""
        # 基于关键词、长度、句式复杂度等
        score = 0.0
        
        # 长度因子
        score += min(len(query) / 500, 0.2)
        
        # 复杂关键词
        complex_keywords = ["分析", "比较", "推理", "计算", "生成", "设计", "优化"]
        for kw in complex_keywords:
            if kw in query:
                score += 0.1
        
        # 多步指示
        if any(w in query for w in ["首先", "然后", "接着", "最后", "第一步"]):
            score += 0.15
        
        # 使用分类模型
        model_score = await self.classifier.predict(query)
        score = score * 0.3 + model_score * 0.7
        
        return min(score, 1.0)
```

---

### 6.2 缓存策略详解

#### 6.2.1 四级缓存架构

```
请求
  |
  v
+-------------------------------------------------------------+
| Level 1: Exact Match Cache (Redis)                         |
| - 完全匹配缓存（query hash）                                 |
| - 命中率：5-10%                                             |
| - 延迟：< 1ms                                               |
| - TTL：1 小时                                               |
+-------------------------------------------------------------+
  | 未命中
  v
+-------------------------------------------------------------+
| Level 2: Semantic Cache (Vector DB)                        |
| - 语义相似度 > 0.95 复用结果                                 |
| - 命中率：15-25%                                            |
| - 延迟：10-20ms                                             |
| - TTL：30 分钟                                              |
+-------------------------------------------------------------+
  | 未命中
  v
+-------------------------------------------------------------+
| Level 3: Prefix Cache (vLLM)                               |
| - 共享前缀 KV Cache                                          |
| - 命中率：20-40%                                            |
| - 延迟：0ms（推理层内部）                                    |
+-------------------------------------------------------------+
  | 未命中
  v
+-------------------------------------------------------------+
| Level 4: Result Cache (Business Logic)                     |
| - 业务结果缓存（如 SQL 查询结果）                            |
| - 命中率：30-50%                                            |
| - TTL：视业务                                               |
+-------------------------------------------------------------+
```

```python
class SemanticCache:
    """语义缓存实现"""
    
    def __init__(self, embedding_model, vector_db, threshold: float = 0.95):
        self.embedding = embedding_model
        self.db = vector_db
        self.threshold = threshold
    
    async def get(self, query: str) -> Optional[str]:
        embedding = await self.embedding.encode(query)
        results = await self.db.search(embedding, top_k=1)
        
        if results and results[0]["score"] > self.threshold:
            return results[0]["payload"]["answer"]
        return None
    
    async def set(self, query: str, answer: str, ttl: int = 1800):
        embedding = await self.embedding.encode(query)
        await self.db.upsert(
            vectors=[embedding],
            metadatas=[{"query": query, "answer": answer, "timestamp": time.time()}],
        )
```

---

### 6.3 请求合并与批处理

```python
class BatchRequestProcessor:
    """动态批处理请求"""
    
    def __init__(self, max_batch_size: int = 16, max_wait_ms: int = 50):
        self.max_batch_size = max_batch_size
        self.max_wait_ms = max_wait_ms
        self.queue = asyncio.Queue()
        self.results = {}
        self._start_processor()
    
    def _start_processor(self):
        asyncio.create_task(self._processor_loop())
    
    async def _processor_loop(self):
        while True:
            batch = []
            start_time = time.time()
            
            # 收集 batch
            while len(batch) < self.max_batch_size:
                elapsed = (time.time() - start_time) * 1000
                remaining = max(0, self.max_wait_ms - elapsed)
                
                try:
                    item = await asyncio.wait_for(self.queue.get(), timeout=remaining / 1000)
                    batch.append(item)
                except asyncio.TimeoutError:
                    break
            
            if batch:
                await self._process_batch(batch)
    
    async def _process_batch(self, batch: list):
        # 合并为批处理请求
        prompts = [item["prompt"] for item in batch]
        
        # 调用模型（批处理）
        results = await self.model.batch_generate(prompts)
        
        # 分发结果
        for item, result in zip(batch, results):
            item["future"].set_result(result)
    
    async def submit(self, prompt: str) -> str:
        future = asyncio.Future()
        await self.queue.put({
            "prompt": prompt,
            "future": future,
        })
        return await future
```

### 6.4 Spot 实例用于推理的策略

```python
class SpotInstanceManager:
    """Spot 实例管理器"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.spot_pools = []
        self.on_demand_fallback = True
    
    async def manage_inference_pods(self):
        """管理推理 Pod 的 Spot 实例"""
        # 1. 核心业务使用 On-Demand
        # 2. 弹性扩容使用 Spot
        # 3. Spot 中断时优雅迁移
        
        # 监听 Spot 中断通知
        while True:
            interruption = await self._wait_for_spot_interruption()
            if interruption:
                await self._graceful_migrate(interruption["node"])
    
    async def _graceful_migrate(self, node_name: str):
        """优雅迁移：先扩容 on-demand，再缩容 spot"""
        # 1. 在 on-demand 节点扩容副本
        await self._scale_up_ondemand(node_name)
        
        # 2. 等待新 Pod Ready
        await self._wait_for_ready(node_name)
        
        # 3. 驱逐 spot 节点上的 Pod
        await self._cordon_and_drain(node_name)
```

### 6.5 成本监控看板设计

```yaml
# Prometheus 成本监控规则
groups:
  - name: llm-cost
    rules:
      - record: llm:cost_per_hour
        expr: |
          sum by (model) (
            llm_requests_total * llm_input_tokens_per_request * llm_input_price_per_token
            + llm_requests_total * llm_output_tokens_per_request * llm_output_price_per_token
          ) * 3600 / 5m
      
      - record: llm:gpu_utilization_cost_efficiency
        expr: |
          llm_tokens_generated_total / (nvidia_gpu_utilization * nvidia_gpu_power_usage)
      
      - alert: HighLLMCost
        expr: llm:cost_per_hour > 100
        for: 5m
        annotations:
          summary: "LLM 成本过高"
          description: "当前 LLM 每小时成本 {{ $value }} 美元"
      
      - alert: LowCacheHitRate
        expr: llm_cache_hits / llm_cache_lookups < 0.1
        for: 10m
        annotations:
          summary: "缓存命中率过低"
          description: "缓存命中率 {{ $value }}，建议优化缓存策略"
```

## 附录：快速参考

### A. 常用命令速查

```bash
# 查看 GPU 利用率
watch -n 1 nvidia-smi

# 查看 Pod 资源使用
kubectl top pod -n ai-platform

# 查看推理服务日志
kubectl logs -f deployment/llm-service -n production --tail=100

# 手动触发 Argo Workflow
argo submit --watch /workflows/retrain.yaml

# 压测命令
locust -f load_test.py --host=http://rag-api:8000 -u 100 -r 10

# 模型导出
python -m transformers.convert_slow_tokenizer checkpoint/
```

### B. 关键配置参数速查

| 参数 | 推荐值 | 说明 |
|------|--------|------|
| vLLM --max-num-seqs | 256 | 最大并发序列数 |
| vLLM --tensor-parallel-size | GPU 数 | 张量并行 |
| vLLM --gpu-memory-utilization | 0.9 | GPU 显存利用率 |
| vLLM --enable-prefix-caching | true | 前缀缓存 |
| Milvus index_type | HNSW | 向量索引类型 |
| Milvus M | 16 | HNSW 参数 |
| Milvus efConstruction | 200 | HNSW 构建参数 |
| LoRA r | 64 | 低秩维度 |
| LoRA alpha | 128 | 缩放因子 |
| LoRA dropout | 0.05 | 丢弃率 |

---

## 八、大模型应用架构

### 8.1 大模型应用的典型架构模式

大模型应用在企业落地时，通常需要面对复杂的业务场景和严苛的性能要求。一个合理且可扩展的架构模式是项目成功的基石。本节将深入剖析四种主流的大模型应用架构模式，从简到繁，逐层递进。

#### 8.1.1 单体直连模式 (Direct API Pattern)

单体直连模式是最简单的大模型应用架构。应用前端直接调用大模型提供的 API（如 OpenAI GPT-4、通义千问等），将所有逻辑（包括 Prompt 工程）封装在前端或一个简单的后端服务中。

**架构图：**

```
+-----------------------------------------------------------+
|                    用户端 (Web/App/小程序)                  |
|  +-------------------+  +-------------------------------+ |
|  | 用户输入模块      |  | 展示模块（流式渲染）          | |
|  +---------+---------+  +---------------+---------------+ |
|            |                            ^                  |
+------------|----------------------------|------------------+
             |                            |
             v                            |
+------------+----------------------------+------------------+
|                    网关层 (API Gateway)                     |
|          限流、鉴权、日志、简单的请求聚合                     |
+------------+----------------------------+------------------+
             |                            |
             v                            |
+------------+----------------+  +--------+-------------------+
|    轻量后端 (可选)            |  |   直接调用                 |
|  Prompt 模板管理              |  |                            |
|  简单的上下文维护              |  |                            |
+------------+----------------+  +--------+-------------------+
             |                            |
             v                            v
+------------+----------------------------+------------------+
|              第三方/自建大模型 API (OpenAI/vLLM)            |
|                   完成 Prompt + 生成响应                    |
+------------------------------------------------------------+
```

**适用场景：**

- 个人开发者或小型团队的 MVP（最小可行产品）阶段
- 内部工具或实验性项目
- 对延迟和成本不敏感的场景（如周报生成、创意文案）
- 流量极低、无并发要求的场景

**优缺点分析：**

| 优点 | 缺点 |
|------|------|
| 开发极快，数小时即可上线 | 无法处理复杂业务逻辑 |
| 架构简单，维护成本低 | 上下文完全依赖模型本身，无法引入私有知识 |
| 无需运维向量数据库等中间件 | 安全性差，Prompt 和 API Key 易泄露 |
| 弹性伸缩由模型供应商提供 | 成本不可控，无法做精细化的流量调度 |
| | 难以做 A/B 测试和模型版本切换 |

**核心代码示例：**

```python
# 单体直连模式的核心实现
import openai
import os
from dataclasses import dataclass

@dataclass
class ChatConfig:
    model: str = "gpt-4o"
    temperature: float = 0.7
    max_tokens: int = 2048
    system_prompt: str = "你是一个有帮助的助手。"

class DirectAPIClient:
    """单体直连模式的客户端实现"""
    
    def __init__(self, config: ChatConfig = None):
        self.config = config or ChatConfig()
        self.client = openai.AsyncOpenAI(api_key=os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY"))
        self.conversation_history = []
    
    async def chat(self, user_message: str) -> str:
        messages = [
            {"role": "system", "content": self.config.system_prompt}
        ] + self.conversation_history + [
            {"role": "user", "content": user_message}
        ]
        
        response = await self.client.chat.completions.create(
            model=self.config.model,
            messages=messages,
            temperature=self.config.temperature,
            max_tokens=self.config.max_tokens,
        )
        
        assistant_message = response.choices[0].message.content
        
        # 维护对话历史（注意：这在生产环境需要更精细的管理）
        self.conversation_history.append({"role": "user", "content": user_message})
        self.conversation_history.append({"role": "assistant", "content": assistant_message})
        
        # 防止历史过长
        if len(self.conversation_history) > 20:
            self.conversation_history = self.conversation_history[-20:]
        
        return assistant_message
    
    def clear_history(self):
        self.conversation_history = []
```

#### 8.1.2 RAG 增强模式 (RAG Pattern)

RAG（Retrieval-Augmented Generation，检索增强生成）是目前企业落地大模型最主流的架构模式。它通过在生成前从外部知识库中检索相关信息，将检索结果作为上下文注入 Prompt，从而显著提升回答的准确性、时效性和可溯源性。

**架构图：**

```
+---------------------------------------------------------------------+
|                            用户请求层                                |
|                    Web / App / API / 第三方系统                       |
+----------------------------+----------------------------------------+
                             |
                             v
+----------------------------+----------------------------------------+
|                          应用服务层 (Application Layer)              |
|  +---------------------+  +---------------------+  +-------------+ |
|  | 会话管理 (Session)  |  | 请求路由 (Router)   |  | 限流/鉴权   | |
|  +----------+----------+  +----------+----------+  +------+------+ |
|             |                        |                    |          |
+-------------|------------------------|--------------------|----------+
              |                        |                    |
              v                        v                    v
+-------------+--------------------------------------------+----------+
|                       RAG 核心处理流水线                               |
|                                                                        |
|  +-------------------+    +-------------------+    +---------------+  |
|  | 查询理解模块      | -> | 检索引擎          | -> | 重排序模块    |  |
|  | - 意图识别        |    | - 向量检索(Dense) |    | - CrossEncoder|  |
|  | - 查询改写        |    | - 关键词检索(Sparse)|   | - 粗排+精排   |  |
|  | - 查询扩展        |    | - 混合检索(Hybrid)|    | - 多样性去重  |  |
|  +-------------------+    +--------+----------+    +-------+-------+  |
|                                    |                       |           |
|                                    v                       v           |
|  +---------------------------------------------------------------+   |
|  |                     Prompt 组装引擎                              |   |
|  |  System Prompt + 检索到的 Top-K 文档 + 用户问题 -> 完整 Prompt   |   |
|  +-------------------------------+--------------------------------+   |
|                                  |                                     |
+----------------------------------|-------------------------------------+
                                   v
+----------------------------------+-------------------------------------+
|                      大模型推理服务 (LLM Service)                      |
|                 vLLM / TensorRT-LLM / 第三方 API                      |
+----------------------------------+-------------------------------------+
                                   |
                                   v
+----------------------------------+-------------------------------------+
|                       后处理与输出层                                   |
|   引用标注 -> 幻觉检测 -> 敏感词过滤 -> 格式化输出 -> 流式返回         |
+------------------------------------------------------------------------+

                           知识库层 (离线)
  +----------+    +----------+    +-----------+    +----------------+
  | 文档采集 | -> | 文档解析 | -> | 分块/Chunk| -> | Embedding 编码 | -> 向量数据库
  +----------+    +----------+    +-----------+    +----------------+
```

**适用场景：**

- 企业知识问答（内部文档、规章制度、产品手册）
- 智能客服（基于历史工单和 FAQ）
- 专业领域助手（法律、医疗、金融合规）
- 内容生成辅助（基于品牌资料的营销文案）

**关键设计要点：**

1. **检索质量决定生成质量**：RAG 系统的上限由检索模块决定。如果检索不到正确的文档片段，再好的大模型也无法生成准确的回答。
2. **上下文窗口的精打细算**：检索结果需要放入有限的上下文窗口中。需要权衡放入文档的数量、每个文档的长度，以及保留多少历史对话。
3. **引用与溯源**：高质量 RAG 系统应支持引用标注，让用户可以验证回答的出处。
4. **多轮对话中的检索**：用户可能在多轮对话中逐步澄清问题，每轮都需要重新检索或基于历史检索结果进行 refine。

#### 8.1.3 Agent 模式 (Agent Pattern)

Agent 模式赋予了模型"行动"的能力。Agent 不仅能生成文本，还能根据任务的复杂程度自主规划、调用工具、观察执行结果，并据此调整下一步行动。这是从"聊天机器人"到"智能助手"的关键跃迁。

**架构图：**

```
+-------------------------------------------------------------------+
|                         Agent 系统架构                              |
+-------------------------------------------------------------------+
|                                                                   |
|  +----------------------------------------------------------------|
|  |                    用户交互层                                     |
|  |  自然语言指令 -> 任务拆解 -> 进度可视化 -> 人工确认节点           |
|  +----------------------------------------------------------------|
|                              |
|                              v
|  +----------------------------------------------------------------|
|  |                    Agent 核心引擎                                 |
|  |                                                                 |
|  |  +----------------+  +----------------+  +------------------+  |
|  |  |   规划模块     |  |   记忆模块     |  |   行动执行器     |  |
|  |  | (Planning)     |  | (Memory)       |  | (Action)         |  |
|  |  |                |  |                |  |                  |  |
|  |  | - ReAct 推理   |  | - 短期记忆     |  | - 工具调用       |  |
|  |  | - Plan-and-Exe |  |   (上下文窗口) |  | - API 调用       |  |
|  |  | - 思维链 (CoT) |  | - 长期记忆     |  | - 代码执行       |  |
|  |  | - 任务分解     |  |   (向量数据库) |  | - 人机协作       |  |
|  |  +--------+-------+  +--------+-------+  +--------+---------+  |
|  |           |                   |                   |            |
|  |           +-------------------+-------------------+            |
|  |                               |                                |
|  |                               v                                |
|  |  +----------------------------------------------------------+ |
|  |  |                LLM 推理核心 (大脑)                         | |
|  |  |   接收：任务状态 + 记忆 + 可用工具列表 -> 输出：下一步行动  | |
|  |  +----------------------------------------------------------+ |
|  +----------------------------------------------------------------|
|                              |
|                              v
|  +----------------------------------------------------------------|
|  |                      工具层 (Tool Layer)                         |
|  |                                                                  |
|  |  +-----------+  +-----------+  +-----------+  +-------------+  |
|  |  | 搜索引擎  |  | 数据库查询|  | 代码解释器|  | 企业 API    |  |
|  |  | (Google/  |  | (SQL/     |  | (Python/  |  | (CRM/ERP/   |  |
|  |  |  Bing)    |  |  NoSQL)   |  |  Shell)   |  |  OA)        |  |
|  |  +-----------+  +-----------+  +-----------+  +-------------+  |
|  |  +-----------+  +-----------+  +-----------+  +-------------+  |
|  |  | 文档工具  |  | 计算工具  |  | 邮件/IM   |  | 第三方 SaaS |  |
|  |  | (RAG检索) |  | (Wolfram) |  | 发送      |  | (Jira/      |  |
|  |  |           |  |           |  |           |  |  GitHub)    |  |
|  |  +-----------+  +-----------+  +-----------+  +-------------+  |
|  +----------------------------------------------------------------|
```

**Agent 的工作循环（ReAct 范式）：**

```
用户输入: "帮我分析一下我们公司 Q3 的销售额趋势，并和去年同期对比"

Thought 1: 用户需要分析销售额趋势和同比数据。我需要：
          1. 查询今年 Q3 的销售数据
          2. 查询去年 Q3 的销售数据
          3. 计算同比变化
          4. 分析趋势并生成报告
Action 1: 调用 [数据库查询工具] 执行 SQL: SELECT * FROM sales WHERE quarter='Q3' AND year=2024

Observation 1: [返回 2024 Q3 销售数据，共 1500 条记录，总金额 4500 万]

Thought 2: 已获得 2024 Q3 数据。现在需要查询 2023 Q3 数据进行同比对比。
Action 2: 调用 [数据库查询工具] 执行 SQL: SELECT SUM(amount) FROM sales WHERE quarter='Q3' AND year=2023

Observation 2: [返回 2023 Q3 总销售额 3800 万]

Thought 3: 已获取两年数据。2024 Q3 = 4500万，2023 Q3 = 3800万。
          同比增长 = (4500 - 3800) / 3800 = 18.4%。
          现在需要获取更多维度数据进行趋势分析。
Action 3: 调用 [数据分析工具] 对 2024 Q3 数据按月分组分析趋势

Observation 3: [返回 7月: 1400万, 8月: 1500万, 9月: 1600万，呈上升趋势]

Thought 4: 数据收集完成。现在可以生成分析报告了。
Action 4: 调用 [报告生成] 整合所有数据，生成带图表的分析报告

Final Answer: [向用户展示完整的分析报告]
```

**适用场景：**

- 复杂数据分析任务（需要多步查询、计算、可视化）
- 自动化办公流程（审批、报表、数据同步）
- 软件开发辅助（需求分析、代码生成、测试、部署）
- 研究与调研（信息搜集、多源对比、报告撰写）

#### 8.1.4 多 Agent 协作模式 (Multi-Agent Pattern)

当业务场景极其复杂、涉及多个专业领域时，单一 Agent 的规划和执行能力会达到瓶颈。多 Agent 协作模式将复杂任务分解给多个专业 Agent，每个 Agent 负责一个子领域，通过明确的通信协议进行协作。这类似于人类团队的工作方式。

**架构图：**

```
+--------------------------------------------------------------------------+
|                      多 Agent 协作系统架构                                 |
+--------------------------------------------------------------------------+
|                                                                          |
|  +---------------------+                                                 |
|  |   用户输入/任务分发  |                                                 |
|  |   (自然语言描述需求) |                                                 |
|  +----------+----------+                                                 |
|             |                                                            |
|             v                                                            |
|  +---------------------+                                                 |
|  |    调度器 (Orchestrator)                                               |
|  |   - 任务分解与分配                                                    |
|  |   - 进度跟踪                                                          |
|  |   - 冲突解决                                                          |
|  |   - 结果汇总                                                          |
|  +----------+----------+----------+----------+----------+                |
|             |          |          |          |          |                |
|             v          v          v          v          v                |
|  +----------+--+ +-----+-----+ +-+---------+ +----------+ +----------+  |
|  | 需求分析Agent| | 技术架构  | | 代码生成  | | 测试Agent | | 文档Agent |  |
```
