```python
        token_embeddings = outputs.last_hidden_state  # [batch, seq_len, hidden_dim]
        
        # L2 归一化
        token_embeddings = torch.nn.functional.normalize(token_embeddings, p=2, dim=-1)
        
        # 按实际长度拆分
        result = []
        for i, text in enumerate(texts):
            attn_mask = inputs["attention_mask"][i]
            valid_len = attn_mask.sum().item()
            result.append(token_embeddings[i, :valid_len])
        
        return result
    
    @torch.no_grad()
    def score(self, query: str, document: str) -> float:
        """计算 ColBERT 风格的 MaxSim 分数"""
        
        # 编码
        q_embeddings = self.encode([query])[0]  # [q_len, dim]
        d_embeddings = self.encode([document])[0]  # [d_len, dim]
        
        # MaxSim: 对每个查询 token，找文档中最相似的 token
        similarity_matrix = torch.matmul(q_embeddings, d_embeddings.T)  # [q_len, d_len]
        max_sims = similarity_matrix.max(dim=1)[0]  # [q_len]
        
        # 求平均（也可求和）
        score = max_sims.mean().item()
        return score
    
    def rerank(self, query: str, documents: list[str]) -> list[dict]:
        """重排序"""
        scores = []
        for doc in documents:
            score = self.score(query, doc)
            scores.append({"document": doc, "score": score})
        
        scores.sort(key=lambda x: x["score"], reverse=True)
        return scores
```

**ColBERT 的优缺点：**

| 优点 | 缺点 |
|------|------|
| 细粒度匹配，效果通常优于 Cross-Encoder | 存储开销大（每个文档存储所有 token 向量） |
| 查询时实时计算，无需像 Cross-Encoder 那样对每个候选做完整前向传播 | 检索阶段计算量较大 |
| 适合长文档 | 实现复杂度较高 |

---

### 9.7 完整 RAG 系统代码

以下是一个生产级 RAG 系统的完整实现，整合了前述所有组件：

```python
"""
Production-Grade RAG System
===========================
一个完整的、模块化的 RAG 系统实现，包含：
- 文档解析与分块
- Embedding 编码与向量存储
- 混合检索 + 重排序
- Prompt 组装与生成
- 引用标注与幻觉检测
"""

import asyncio
import hashlib
import time
from dataclasses import dataclass, field
from typing import List, Optional, Dict, Any, Callable
from datetime import datetime
import numpy as np

# ==================== 数据模型 ====================

@dataclass
class Document:
    """文档模型"""
    id: str
    content: str
    metadata: Dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
    source: str = ""
    created_at: datetime = field(default_factory=datetime.now)

@dataclass
class Chunk:
    """文档块模型"""
    id: str
    document_id: str
    content: str
    index: int
    start: int
    end: int
    metadata: Dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)

@dataclass
class RetrievedChunk:
    """检索结果模型"""
    chunk: Chunk
    score: float
    retrieval_method: str  # "dense", "sparse", "hybrid"

@dataclass
class RAGResponse:
    """RAG 响应模型"""
    answer: str
    sources: List[RetrievedChunk]
    citations: List[Dict[str, Any]]
    latency_ms: float
    tokens_used: Dict[str, int]
    metadata: Dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)

# ==================== 分块模块 ====================

class ChunkingEngine:
    """分块引擎"""
    
    def __init__(self, chunk_size: int = 512, chunk_overlap: int = 50, strategy: str = "recursive"):
        self.chunk_size = chunk_size
        self.chunk_overlap = chunk_overlap
        self.strategy = strategy
    
    def chunk_document(self, document: Document) -> List[Chunk]:
        """对文档进行分块"""
        if self.strategy == "recursive":
            raw_chunks = self._recursive_split(document.content)
        elif self.strategy == "fixed":
            raw_chunks = self._fixed_split(document.content)
        else:
            raw_chunks = self._fixed_split(document.content)
        
        chunks = []
        for i, (content, start, end) in enumerate(raw_chunks):
            chunk_id = f"{document.id}_chunk_{i}"
            chunks.append(Chunk(
                id=chunk_id,
                document_id=document.id,
                content=content,
                index=i,
                start=start,
                end=end,
                metadata=document.metadata.copy(),
            ))
        return chunks
    
    def _recursive_split(self, text: str) -> List[tuple]:
        """递归分块"""
        separators = ["\n\n\n", "\n\n", "\n", "。", "；", "，", " ", ""]
        return self._split_with_separators(text, separators, 0)
    
    def _split_with_separators(self, text: str, separators: List[str], sep_idx: int) -> List[tuple]:
        if len(text) <= self.chunk_size or sep_idx >= len(separators):
            return [(text.strip(), 0, len(text))] if text.strip() else []
        
        sep = separators[sep_idx]
        if sep == "":
            return self._fixed_split(text)
        
        parts = text.split(sep)
        chunks = []
        current = ""
        current_start = 0
        
        for part in parts:
            candidate = current + sep + part if current else part
            if len(candidate) <= self.chunk_size:
                current = candidate
            else:
                if current.strip():
                    if len(current) > self.chunk_size * 1.5:
                        chunks.extend(self._split_with_separators(current, separators, sep_idx + 1))
                    else:
                        chunks.append((current.strip(), current_start, current_start + len(current)))
                current = part
                current_start = text.find(part, current_start)
        
        if current.strip():
            if len(current) > self.chunk_size * 1.5:
                chunks.extend(self._split_with_separators(current, separators, sep_idx + 1))
            else:
                chunks.append((current.strip(), current_start, current_start + len(current)))
        
        return chunks
    
    def _fixed_split(self, text: str) -> List[tuple]:
        """固定长度分块"""
        chunks = []
        start = 0
        while start < len(text):
            end = min(start + self.chunk_size, len(text))
            if end < len(text):
                for s in ["\n\n", "。", ". ", "\n"]:
                    pos = text.rfind(s, start, end)
                    if pos > start + self.chunk_size * 0.5:
                        end = pos + len(s)
                        break
            chunk_text = text[start:end].strip()
            if chunk_text:
                chunks.append((chunk_text, start, end))
            start = end - self.chunk_overlap if end < len(text) else end
        return chunks

# ==================== Embedding 模块 ====================

class EmbeddingEngine:
    """Embedding 引擎"""
    
    def __init__(self, model_name: str = "BAAI/bge-large-zh-v1.5", device: str = "cuda", batch_size: int = 32):
        from sentence_transformers import SentenceTransformer
        self.model = SentenceTransformer(model_name, device=device)
        self.batch_size = batch_size
        self.dim = self.model.get_sentence_embedding_dimension()
    
    def encode(self, texts: List[str]) -> np.ndarray:
        """编码文本"""
        embeddings = self.model.encode(
            texts,
            batch_size=self.batch_size,
            show_progress_bar=False,
            normalize_embeddings=True,
        )
        return embeddings

# ==================== 向量存储模块 ====================

class VectorStore:
    """向量存储抽象"""
    
    def __init__(self, collection_name: str, dim: int):
        self.collection_name = collection_name
        self.dim = dim
        self.vectors: Dict[str, np.ndarray] = {}
        self.documents: Dict[str, str] = {}
        self.metadatas: Dict[str, Dict] = {}
    
    def add(self, ids: List[str], embeddings: np.ndarray, documents: List[str], metadatas: List[Dict]):
        """添加向量"""
        for i, id in enumerate(ids):
            self.vectors[id] = embeddings[i]
            self.documents[id] = documents[i]
            self.metadatas[id] = metadatas[i]
    
    def search(self, query_embedding: np.ndarray, top_k: int = 10, filter_fn: Callable = None) -> List[tuple]:
        """向量搜索（简化版：暴力计算）"""
        scores = []
        for id, vec in self.vectors.items():
            if filter_fn and not filter_fn(self.metadatas[id]):
                continue
            sim = np.dot(query_embedding, vec)
            scores.append((id, float(sim)))
        scores.sort(key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)
        return scores[:top_k]
    
    def delete(self, ids: List[str]):
        """删除向量"""
        for id in ids:
            self.vectors.pop(id, None)
            self.documents.pop(id, None)
            self.metadatas.pop(id, None)

# ==================== 检索模块 ====================

class RetrievalEngine:
    """检索引擎"""
    
    def __init__(
        self,
        vector_store: VectorStore,
        embedding_engine: EmbeddingEngine,
        reranker = None,
        top_k_dense: int = 50,
        top_k_final: int = 5,
    ):
        self.vector_store = vector_store
        self.embedding_engine = embedding_engine
        self.reranker = reranker
        self.top_k_dense = top_k_dense
        self.top_k_final = top_k_final
    
    async def retrieve(self, query: str, chunk_map: Dict[str, Chunk], filter_fn: Callable = None) -> List[RetrievedChunk]:
        """执行检索"""
        start_time = time.time()
        
        # 1. Dense 检索
        query_embedding = self.embedding_engine.encode([query])[0]
        dense_results = self.vector_store.search(query_embedding, top_k=self.top_k_dense, filter_fn=filter_fn)
        
        retrieved = [
            RetrievedChunk(
                chunk=chunk_map[id],
                score=score,
                retrieval_method="dense",
            )
            for id, score in dense_results if id in chunk_map
        ]
        
        # 2. 重排序（如果有）
        if self.reranker and retrieved:
            docs = [r.chunk.content for r in retrieved]
            reranked = self.reranker.rerank(query, docs)
            
            # 更新分数
            score_map = {r["document"]: r["score"] for r in reranked}
            for r in retrieved:
                if r.chunk.content in score_map:
                    r.score = score_map[r.chunk.content]
                    r.retrieval_method = "dense+rerank"
            
            retrieved.sort(key=lambda x: x.score, reverse=True)
        
        return retrieved[:self.top_k_final]

# ==================== Prompt 模块 ====================

class PromptEngine:
    """Prompt 引擎"""
    
    def __init__(
        self,
        system_template: str = None,
        context_template: str = None,
        citation_template: str = None,
        max_context_tokens: int = 3000,
    ):
        self.system_template = system_template or (
            "你是一个专业的助手。请基于以下参考文档回答用户问题。"
            "如果参考文档中没有相关信息，请明确说明。"
            "回答时请标注引用来源，格式为 [^index^]。"
        )
        self.context_template = context_template or "[^{index}^] {content}\n"
        self.citation_template = citation_template or "[^{index}^] 来源: {source}"
        self.max_context_tokens = max_context_tokens
    
    def build_prompt(self, query: str, retrieved_chunks: List[RetrievedChunk]) -> tuple:
        """构建 Prompt"""
        
        # 组装上下文
        context_parts = []
        total_chars = 0
        max_chars = self.max_context_tokens * 3  # 粗略估算
        
        used_chunks = []
        for i, chunk in enumerate(retrieved_chunks):
            part = self.context_template.format(index=i + 1, content=chunk.chunk.content)
            if total_chars + len(part) > max_chars:
                break
            context_parts.append(part)
            used_chunks.append(chunk)
            total_chars += len(part)
        
        context = "".join(context_parts)
        
        prompt = f"""{self.system_template}

参考文档：
{context}

用户问题：{query}

请基于参考文档回答，并标注引用来源。"""
        
        return prompt, used_chunks
    
    def extract_citations(self, answer: str, used_chunks: List[RetrievedChunk]) -> List[Dict]:
        """提取回答中的引用"""
        import re
        citations = []
        
        pattern = r'\[\^(\d+)\^\]'
        matches = re.finditer(pattern, answer)
        
        for match in matches:
            idx = int(match.group(1)) - 1
            if 0 <= idx < len(used_chunks):
                chunk = used_chunks[idx]
                citations.append({
                    "index": idx + 1,
                    "document_id": chunk.chunk.document_id,
                    "content_preview": chunk.chunk.content[:200],
                    "score": chunk.score,
                })
        
        return citations

# ==================== 幻觉检测模块 ====================

class HallucinationDetector:
    """幻觉检测器"""
    
    def __init__(self, embedding_engine: EmbeddingEngine = None, threshold: float = 0.6):
        self.embedding_engine = embedding_engine
        self.threshold = threshold
    
    def detect(self, answer: str, retrieved_chunks: List[RetrievedChunk]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """检测幻觉"""
        
        if not self.embedding_engine or not retrieved_chunks:
            return {"hallucination_detected": False, "confidence": 0}
        
        # 将回答分句
        sentences = self._split_sentences(answer)
        
        # 编码所有参考文档
        ref_texts = [c.chunk.content for c in retrieved_chunks]
        ref_embeddings = self.embedding_engine.encode(ref_texts)
        
        suspicious_sentences = []
        
        for sent in sentences:
            if len(sent) < 10:
                continue
            
            sent_embedding = self.embedding_engine.encode([sent])[0]
            
            # 计算与每个参考文档的最大相似度
            max_sim = max(np.dot(sent_embedding, ref_emb) for ref_emb in ref_embeddings)
            
            if max_sim < self.threshold:
                suspicious_sentences.append({
                    "sentence": sent,
                    "max_similarity": float(max_sim),
                })
        
        hallucination_ratio = len(suspicious_sentences) / max(len(sentences), 1)
        
        return {
            "hallucination_detected": hallucination_ratio > 0.3,
            "hallucination_ratio": hallucination_ratio,
            "suspicious_sentences": suspicious_sentences,
            "confidence": 1 - hallucination_ratio,
        }
    
    def _split_sentences(self, text: str) -> List[str]:
        import re
        pattern = r'[^。！？.?!\n]+[。！？.?!\n]*'
        return [s.strip() for s in re.findall(pattern, text) if s.strip()]

# ==================== 主 RAG 系统 ====================

class RAGSystem:
    """完整 RAG 系统"""
    
    def __init__(
        self,
        embedding_engine: EmbeddingEngine,
        llm_client,
        reranker = None,
        chunk_size: int = 512,
        chunk_overlap: int = 50,
        top_k_dense: int = 50,
        top_k_final: int = 5,
    ):
        self.embedding_engine = embedding_engine
        self.llm = llm_client
        self.reranker = reranker
        
        self.chunking_engine = ChunkingEngine(chunk_size=chunk_size, chunk_overlap=chunk_overlap)
        self.vector_store: Optional[VectorStore] = None
        self.retrieval_engine: Optional[RetrievalEngine] = None
        self.prompt_engine = PromptEngine()
        self.hallucination_detector = HallucinationDetector(embedding_engine)
        
        self.chunk_map: Dict[str, Chunk] = {}
        self.document_map: Dict[str, Document] = {}
    
    def initialize_store(self, collection_name: str = "rag_collection"):
        """初始化向量存储"""
        self.vector_store = VectorStore(collection_name, self.embedding_engine.dim)
        self.retrieval_engine = RetrievalEngine(
            vector_store=self.vector_store,
            embedding_engine=self.embedding_engine,
            reranker=self.reranker,
            top_k_dense=50,
            top_k_final=5,
        )
    
    async def index_documents(self, documents: List[Document]):
        """索引文档"""
        all_chunks = []
        
        for doc in documents:
            self.document_map[doc.id] = doc
            chunks = self.chunking_engine.chunk_document(doc)
            for chunk in chunks:
                self.chunk_map[chunk.id] = chunk
                all_chunks.append(chunk)
        
        # 批量编码
        batch_size = 64
        for i in range(0, len(all_chunks), batch_size):
            batch = all_chunks[i:i + batch_size]
            texts = [c.content for c in batch]
            embeddings = self.embedding_engine.encode(texts)
            
            self.vector_store.add(
                ids=[c.id for c in batch],
                embeddings=embeddings,
                documents=[c.content for c in batch],
                metadatas=[{
                    "document_id": c.document_id,
                    "index": c.index,
                    **c.metadata,
                } for c in batch],
            )
    
    async def query(self, query: str, filter_fn: Callable = None) -> RAGResponse:
        """执行 RAG 查询"""
        start_time = time.time()
        
        # 1. 检索
        retrieved = await self.retrieval_engine.retrieve(query, self.chunk_map, filter_fn)
        
        # 2. 构建 Prompt
        prompt, used_chunks = self.prompt_engine.build_prompt(query, retrieved)
        
        # 3. 生成回答
        response = await self.llm.generate(prompt)
        answer = response.get("content", "")
        
        # 4. 提取引用
        citations = self.prompt_engine.extract_citations(answer, used_chunks)
        
        # 5. 幻觉检测
        hallucination = self.hallucination_detector.detect(answer, used_chunks)
        
        latency_ms = (time.time() - start_time) * 1000
        
        return RAGResponse(
            answer=answer,
            sources=used_chunks,
            citations=citations,
            latency_ms=latency_ms,
            tokens_used={"input": len(prompt) // 3, "output": len(answer) // 3},
            metadata={
                "hallucination": hallucination,
                "num_sources": len(used_chunks),
            },
        )

# ==================== 使用示例 ====================

async def main():
    """RAG 系统使用示例"""
    
    # 初始化组件
    embedding_engine = EmbeddingEngine("BAAI/bge-large-zh-v1.5")
    
    # LLM 客户端（需要实现）
    class SimpleLLM:
        async def generate(self, prompt: str, **kwargs):
            # 这里接入实际的 LLM API
            return {"content": f"基于文档的回答：这是关于 '{prompt[:30]}...' 的模拟回答 [^1^]。"}
    
    llm = SimpleLLM()
    
    # 初始化 RAG 系统
    rag = RAGSystem(
        embedding_engine=embedding_engine,
        llm_client=llm,
        chunk_size=512,
        chunk_overlap=50,
    )
    rag.initialize_store("demo")
    
    # 准备文档
    docs = [
        Document(id="doc_1", content="大模型应用架构设计需要考虑扩展性、可靠性和成本。", source="架构指南"),
        Document(id="doc_2", content="RAG 系统通过检索增强生成来提升回答准确性。", source="RAG 白皮书"),
        Document(id="doc_3", content="向量数据库用于存储和检索高维向量。", source="技术文档"),
    ]
    
    # 索引
    await rag.index_documents(docs)
    
    # 查询
    result = await rag.query("什么是 RAG 系统？")
    print(f"回答：{result.answer}")
    print(f"来源数：{len(result.sources)}")
    print(f"延迟：{result.latency_ms:.1f}ms")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    asyncio.run(main())
```

---

### 9.8 RAG 评估框架

RAG 系统的优化需要可量化的评估指标。RAGAS 和 Ares 是目前最常用的两个评估框架。

#### 9.8.1 RAGAS（RAG Assessment）

RAGAS 是一个无需人工标注的 RAG 评估框架，利用 LLM 自动评估以下指标：

| 指标 | 说明 | 计算公式 |
|------|------|----------|
| **Faithfulness** | 回答是否忠实于检索到的上下文 | 回答中可由上下文支撑的事实数 / 总事实数 |
| **Answer Relevancy** | 回答与问题的相关程度 | 基于生成问题的相似度计算 |
| **Context Precision** | 检索到的上下文中相关块的比例 | 相关块数 / 总检索块数 |
| **Context Recall** | 是否检索到了回答问题所需的所有信息 | 回答中事实对应的上下文块比例 |
| **Context Relevancy** | 检索到的上下文与问题的相关程度 | 相关句子数 / 总句子数 |

```python
# RAGAS 使用示例
from ragas import evaluate
from ragas.metrics import (
    faithfulness,
    answer_relevancy,
    context_precision,
    context_recall,
    context_relevancy,
)
from datasets import Dataset

class RAGASEvaluator:
    """RAGAS 评估器"""
    
    def __init__(self, llm_client):
        self.llm = llm_client
    
    def evaluate(self, queries: list[str], answers: list[str], contexts: list[list[str]], 
                 ground_truths: list[str] = None) -> dict:
        """评估 RAG 系统"""
        
        data = {
            "question": queries,
            "answer": answers,
            "contexts": contexts,
        }
        if ground_truths:
            data["ground_truth"] = ground_truths
        
        dataset = Dataset.from_dict(data)
        
        metrics = [faithfulness, answer_relevancy, context_precision, context_recall]
        if ground_truths:
            metrics.append(context_relevancy)
        
        result = evaluate(
            dataset=dataset,
            metrics=metrics,
        )
        
        return result.to_pandas().to_dict()
    
    def custom_faithfulness(self, answer: str, contexts: list[str]) -> float:
        """自定义忠实度计算"""
        # 让 LLM 判断回答中的每个事实是否能在上下文中找到支撑
        prompt = f"""请判断以下回答中的每个事实是否都能在给定的上下文中找到依据。

上下文：
{"\n".join(contexts)}

回答：{answer}

请按以下格式输出：
事实1: [在上下文中找到/未找到]
事实2: [在上下文中找到/未找到]
...

忠实度评分 = 找到依据的事实数 / 总事实数

请只输出最后的评分（0-1 之间的小数）。"""
        
        response = self.llm.generate(prompt)
        try:
            score = float(response.strip())
            return max(0, min(1, score))
        except:
            return 0.5
```

#### 9.8.2 Ares（Automatic RAG Evaluation System）

Ares 是一个全自动的 RAG 评估系统，通过合成数据训练专门的评估模型。

```python
class ARESRAGEvaluator:
    """ARES 风格评估器（简化概念）"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.context_relevance_classifier = None
        self.answer_faithfulness_classifier = None
        self.answer_relevance_classifier = None
    
    def prepare_synthetic_data(self, documents: list[str], num_queries: int = 100) -> list[dict]:
        """生成合成评估数据"""
        # 1. 从文档中采样段落
        # 2. 用 LLM 生成基于段落的问题和答案
        # 3. 构造正负样本（正确答案 + 错误答案）
        synthetic_data = []
        
        for doc in documents:
            # 生成问题
            prompt = f"""基于以下文档段落，生成 3 个问题及其答案：

文档：{doc[:1000]}

格式：
Q1: [问题]
A1: [答案]

Q2: ..."""
            
            # 这里需要调用 LLM
            # synthetic_data.extend(parse_qa_pairs(response))
        
        return synthetic_data
    
    def train_classifiers(self, synthetic_data: list[dict]):
        """训练评估分类器（使用 BERT 等轻量模型）"""
        # 实际实现需要使用 transformers 库训练分类器
        pass
    
    def evaluate(self, query: str, contexts: list[str], answer: str) -> dict:
        """评估单个查询"""
        return {
            "context_relevance": 0.85,  # 由分类器预测
            "answer_faithfulness": 0.92,
            "answer_relevance": 0.88,
        }
```

#### 9.8.3 评估实施建议

```python
class RAGEvaluationPipeline:
    """RAG 评估流水线"""
    
    def __init__(self, rag_system, test_dataset: list[dict]):
        self.rag = rag_system
        self.test_dataset = test_dataset
    
    async def run(self) -> dict:
        """运行完整评估"""
        results = {
            "queries": [],
            "answers": [],
            "contexts": [],
            "ground_truths": [],
            "latencies": [],
        }
        
        for item in self.test_dataset:
            query = item["question"]
            start = time.time()
            response = await self.rag.query(query)
            latency = (time.time() - start) * 1000
            
            results["queries"].append(query)
            results["answers"].append(response.answer)
            results["contexts"].append([c.chunk.content for c in response.sources])
            results["ground_truths"].append(item.get("ground_truth", ""))
            results["latencies"].append(latency)
        
        # RAGAS 评估
        ragas_scores = self._ragas_evaluate(results)
        
        # 自定义指标
        custom_scores = {
            "avg_latency_ms": sum(results["latencies"]) / len(results["latencies"]),
            "p95_latency_ms": sorted(results["latencies"])[int(len(results["latencies"]) * 0.95)],
            "avg_sources_used": sum(len(c) for c in results["contexts"]) / len(results["contexts"]),
        }
        
        return {**ragas_scores, **custom_scores}
    
    def _ragas_evaluate(self, results: dict) -> dict:
        # 调用 RAGAS 进行评估
        return {}
```

**RAG 评估指标目标值参考：**

| 指标 | 入门 | 良好 | 优秀 |
|------|------|------|------|
| Faithfulness | > 0.6 | > 0.75 | > 0.85 |
| Answer Relevancy | > 0.6 | > 0.75 | > 0.85 |
| Context Precision | > 0.5 | > 0.7 | > 0.85 |
| Context Recall | > 0.5 | > 0.7 | > 0.85 |
| 平均延迟 | < 3s | < 1.5s | < 800ms |

# 第四部分：RAG 系统完整实现

---

## 第16章 RAG 系统从零构建

### 16.1 完整 RAG 架构实现

#### 系统架构

```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                        RAG 系统架构                              │
│                                                                  │
│  输入层                                                           │
│  ├── 文档摄取（PDF/Word/HTML/Markdown）                           │
│  ├── 文档解析（OCR/表格/图片）                                    │
│  └── 数据清洗（去重/去噪/格式统一）                               │
│                                                                  │
│  处理层                                                           │
│  ├── 文本分块（Chunking）                                        │
│  ├── 文本增强（摘要/关键词/元数据）                               │
│  └── 向量化（Embedding）                                         │
│                                                                  │
│  存储层                                                           │
│  ├── 向量数据库（Milvus/Pinecone/Weaviate）                       │
│  ├── 倒排索引（Elasticsearch）                                    │
│  └── 缓存层（Redis）                                             │
│                                                                  │
│  检索层                                                           │
│  ├── 向量检索（相似度搜索）                                       │
│  ├── 关键词检索（BM25）                                          │
│  ├── 混合检索（向量+关键词）                                      │
│  └── 重排序（Reranker）                                          │
│                                                                  │
│  生成层                                                           │
│  ├── 查询改写（Query Rewriting）                                 │
│  ├── Prompt 构建（上下文组装）                                    │
│  └── LLM 生成                                                    │
│                                                                  │
│  输出层                                                           │
│  ├── 答案生成                                                    │
│  ├── 引用标注（Source Attribution）                              │
│  └── 后处理（格式化/过滤）                                        │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

#### 完整代码实现

```python
# rag_system.py
import os
import hashlib
from typing import List, Dict, Optional, Tuple
from dataclasses import dataclass
import numpy as np
import torch
from transformers import AutoTokenizer, AutoModel
from langchain.text_splitter import RecursiveCharacterTextSplitter
from langchain.document_loaders import (
    PyPDFLoader, 
    UnstructuredWordDocumentLoader,
    UnstructuredHTMLLoader
)
from pymilvus import (
    connections, 
    FieldSchema, 
    CollectionSchema, 
    DataType,
    Collection,
    utility
)
import redis
from rank_bm25 import BM25Okapi
import jieba

@dataclass
class Document:
    """文档数据结构"""
    id: str
    content: str
    metadata: Dict
    embedding: Optional[np.ndarray] = None

@dataclass
class RetrievedChunk:
    """检索到的块"""
    content: str
    score: float
    metadata: Dict
    retrieval_method: str  # "vector" or "bm25"

class DocumentProcessor:
    """文档处理器"""
    
    def __init__(self, chunk_size=512, chunk_overlap=50):
        self.chunk_size = chunk_size
        self.chunk_overlap = chunk_overlap
        self.text_splitter = RecursiveCharacterTextSplitter(
            chunk_size=chunk_size,
            chunk_overlap=chunk_overlap,
            length_function=len,
            separators=["\n\n", "\n", "。", "；", "，", " ", ""]
        )
    
    def load_document(self, file_path: str) -> List[Document]:
        """加载文档"""
        ext = os.path.splitext(file_path)[1].lower()
        
        if ext == '.pdf':
            loader = PyPDFLoader(file_path)
        elif ext in ['.doc', '.docx']:
            loader = UnstructuredWordDocumentLoader(file_path)
        elif ext in ['.html', '.htm']:
            loader = UnstructuredHTMLLoader(file_path)
        else:
            with open(file_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                content = f.read()
            return [self._create_document(content, {"source": file_path})]
        
        docs = loader.load()
        return [
            self._create_document(doc.page_content, doc.metadata)
            for doc in docs
        ]
    
    def _create_document(self, content: str, metadata: Dict) -> Document:
        doc_id = hashlib.md5(content.encode()).hexdigest()
        return Document(
            id=doc_id,
            content=content,
            metadata=metadata
        )
    
    def split_documents(self, documents: List[Document]) -> List[Document]:
        """分块处理"""
        chunks = []
        for doc in documents:
            texts = self.text_splitter.split_text(doc.content)
            for i, text in enumerate(texts):
                chunk_id = f"{doc.id}_{i}"
                chunks.append(Document(
                    id=chunk_id,
                    content=text,
                    metadata={
                        **doc.metadata,
                        "chunk_index": i,
                        "parent_id": doc.id
                    }
                ))
        return chunks
    
    def enhance_chunks(self, chunks: List[Document]) -> List[Document]:
        """块增强：添加摘要和关键词"""
        enhanced = []
        for chunk in chunks:
            # 生成摘要（前 100 字）
            summary = chunk.content[:100] + "..."
            
            # 提取关键词（简单实现）
            words = jieba.lcut(chunk.content)
            keywords = [w for w in words if len(w) > 1][:5]
            
            chunk.metadata["summary"] = summary
            chunk.metadata["keywords"] = ",".join(keywords)
            enhanced.append(chunk)
        
        return enhanced

class EmbeddingModel:
    """Embedding 模型"""
    
    def __init__(self, model_name="BAAI/bge-large-zh-v1.5"):
        self.device = "cuda" if torch.cuda.is_available() else "cpu"
        self.tokenizer = AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained(model_name)
        self.model = AutoModel.from_pretrained(model_name).to(self.device)
        self.model.eval()
        self.max_length = 512
    
    def encode(self, texts: List[str], batch_size=32) -> np.ndarray:
        """编码文本为向量"""
        embeddings = []
        
        for i in range(0, len(texts), batch_size):
            batch = texts[i:i+batch_size]
            
            inputs = self.tokenizer(
                batch,
                padding=True,
                truncation=True,
                max_length=self.max_length,
                return_tensors="pt"
            ).to(self.device)
            
            with torch.no_grad():
                outputs = self.model(**inputs)
                # 使用 CLS token 的 embedding
                batch_embeddings = outputs.last_hidden_state[:, 0].cpu().numpy()
                # 归一化
                batch_embeddings = batch_embeddings / np.linalg.norm(
                    batch_embeddings, axis=1, keepdims=True
                )
            
            embeddings.append(batch_embeddings)
        
        return np.vstack(embeddings)

class VectorStore:
    """向量数据库封装"""
    
    def __init__(self, collection_name="rag_collection", dim=1024):
        self.collection_name = collection_name
        self.dim = dim
        self._connect()
        self._create_collection()
    
    def _connect(self):
        connections.connect(
            alias="default",
            host=os.getenv("MILVUS_HOST", "localhost"),
            port=os.getenv("MILVUS_PORT", "19530")
        )
    
    def _create_collection(self):
        if utility.has_collection(self.collection_name):
            self.collection = Collection(self.collection_name)
            return
        
        fields = [
            FieldSchema(name="id", dtype=DataType.VARCHAR, max_length=64, is_primary=True),
            FieldSchema(name="content", dtype=DataType.VARCHAR, max_length=65535),
            FieldSchema(name="embedding", dtype=DataType.FLOAT_VECTOR, dim=self.dim),
            FieldSchema(name="metadata", dtype=DataType.VARCHAR, max_length=4096),
        ]
        
        schema = CollectionSchema(fields, self.collection_name)
        self.collection = Collection(self.collection_name, schema)
        
        # 创建索引
        index_params = {
            "metric_type": "COSINE",
            "index_type": "HNSW",
            "params": {"M": 16, "efConstruction": 200}
        }
        self.collection.create_index("embedding", index_params)
        self.collection.load()
    
    def insert(self, chunks: List[Document]):
        """插入文档块"""
        entities = [
            [c.id for c in chunks],
            [c.content for c in chunks],
            [c.embedding.tolist() for c in chunks],
            [str(c.metadata) for c in chunks]
        ]
        self.collection.insert(entities)
        self.collection.flush()
    
    def search(self, query_embedding: np.ndarray, top_k=10) -> List[RetrievedChunk]:
        """向量检索"""
        search_params = {"metric_type": "COSINE", "params": {"ef": 64}}
        
        results = self.collection.search(
            data=[query_embedding.tolist()],
            anns_field="embedding",
            param=search_params,
            limit=top_k,
            output_fields=["content", "metadata"]
        )
        
        chunks = []
        for result in results[0]:
            chunks.append(RetrievedChunk(
                content=result.entity.get("content"),
                score=result.distance,
                metadata=eval(result.entity.get("metadata")),
                retrieval_method="vector"
            ))
        return chunks

class BM25Retriever:
    """BM25 关键词检索"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.corpus = []
        self.bm25 = None
        self.chunk_map = {}
    
    def build_index(self, chunks: List[Document]):
        """构建 BM25 索引"""
        self.corpus = []
        for chunk in chunks:
            # 中文分词
            tokens = jieba.lcut(chunk.content)
            self.corpus.append(tokens)
            self.chunk_map[len(self.corpus)-1] = chunk
        
        self.bm25 = BM25Okapi(self.corpus)
    
    def search(self, query: str, top_k=10) -> List[RetrievedChunk]:
        """BM25 检索"""
        query_tokens = jieba.lcut(query)
        scores = self.bm25.get_scores(query_tokens)
        
        # 获取 top-k
        top_indices = np.argsort(scores)[::-1][:top_k]
        
        results = []
        for idx in top_indices:
            if scores[idx] > 0:
                chunk = self.chunk_map[idx]
                results.append(RetrievedChunk(
                    content=chunk.content,
                    score=float(scores[idx]),
                    metadata=chunk.metadata,
                    retrieval_method="bm25"
                ))
        return results

class Reranker:
    """重排序模型"""
    
    def __init__(self, model_name="BAAI/bge-reranker-large"):
        self.device = "cuda" if torch.cuda.is_available() else "cpu"
        self.tokenizer = AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained(model_name)
        self.model = AutoModel.from_pretrained(model_name).to(self.device)
        self.model.eval()
    
    def rerank(self, query: str, chunks: List[RetrievedChunk], top_k=5) -> List[RetrievedChunk]:
        """对检索结果重排序"""
        pairs = [(query, chunk.content) for chunk in chunks]
        
        scores = []
        for query_text, doc_text in pairs:
            inputs = self.tokenizer(
                query_text, doc_text,
                padding=True,
                truncation=True,
                max_length=512,
                return_tensors="pt"
            ).to(self.device)
            
            with torch.no_grad():
                outputs = self.model(**inputs)
                score = outputs.logits[0][0].cpu().item()
            
            scores.append(score)
        
        # 按分数排序
        sorted_indices = np.argsort(scores)[::-1]
        
        results = []
        for idx in sorted_indices[:top_k]:
            chunk = chunks[idx]
            chunk.score = scores[idx]
            results.append(chunk)
        
        return results

class RAGSystem:
    """完整 RAG 系统"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.doc_processor = DocumentProcessor()
        self.embedding_model = EmbeddingModel()
        self.vector_store = VectorStore()
        self.bm25_retriever = BM25Retriever()
        self.reranker = Reranker()
        self.redis_cache = redis.Redis(
            host=os.getenv("REDIS_HOST", "localhost"),
            port=int(os.getenv("REDIS_PORT", "6379")),
            db=0
        )
    
    def ingest_documents(self, file_paths: List[str]):
        """摄入文档"""
        all_chunks = []
        
        for file_path in file_paths:
            print(f"Processing {file_path}...")
            docs = self.doc_processor.load_document(file_path)
            chunks = self.doc_processor.split_documents(docs)
            chunks = self.doc_processor.enhance_chunks(chunks)
            all_chunks.extend(chunks)
        
        # 生成 embedding
        print("Generating embeddings...")
        texts = [c.content for c in all_chunks]
        embeddings = self.embedding_model.encode(texts)
        
        for i, chunk in enumerate(all_chunks):
            chunk.embedding = embeddings[i]
        
        # 存入向量数据库
        print("Storing in vector database...")
        self.vector_store.insert(all_chunks)
        
        # 构建 BM25 索引
        print("Building BM25 index...")
        self.bm25_retriever.build_index(all_chunks)
        
        print(f"Ingested {len(all_chunks)} chunks from {len(file_paths)} documents")
    
    def retrieve(self, query: str, top_k=10, use_rerank=True) -> List[RetrievedChunk]:
        """检索"""
        # 检查缓存
        cache_key = f"rag:retrieve:{hashlib.md5(query.encode()).hexdigest()}"
        cached = self.redis_cache.get(cache_key)
        if cached:
            # 反序列化缓存结果
            pass
        
        # 1. 向量检索
        query_embedding = self.embedding_model.encode([query])[0]
        vector_results = self.vector_store.search(query_embedding, top_k=top_k)
        
        # 2. BM25 检索
        bm25_results = self.bm25_retriever.search(query, top_k=top_k)
        
        # 3. 融合结果（Reciprocal Rank Fusion）
        fused = self._reciprocal_rank_fusion(vector_results, bm25_results)
        
        # 4. 重排序
        if use_rerank:
            fused = self.reranker.rerank(query, fused, top_k=top_k)
        
        # 缓存结果
        # self.redis_cache.setex(cache_key, 3600, serialize(fused))
        
        return fused
    
    def _reciprocal_rank_fusion(self, vector_results: List[RetrievedChunk], 
                                 bm25_results: List[RetrievedChunk],
                                 k=60) -> List[RetrievedChunk]:
        """RRF 融合算法"""
        scores = {}
        
        for rank, result in enumerate(vector_results):
            if result.content not in scores:
                scores[result.content] = {"score": 0, "metadata": result.metadata}
            scores[result.content]["score"] += 1 / (k + rank + 1)
        
        for rank, result in enumerate(bm25_results):
            if result.content not in scores:
                scores[result.content] = {"score": 0, "metadata": result.metadata}
            scores[result.content]["score"] += 1 / (k + rank + 1)
        
        # 排序
        sorted_items = sorted(scores.items(), key=lambda x: x[1]["score"], reverse=True)
        
        return [
            RetrievedChunk(
                content=content,
                score=data["score"],
                metadata=data["metadata"],
                retrieval_method="hybrid"
            )
            for content, data in sorted_items
        ]
    
    def generate(self, query: str, llm_client, top_k=5) -> Dict:
        """生成答案"""
        # 1. 检索相关文档
        retrieved = self.retrieve(query, top_k=top_k)
        
        # 2. 构建上下文
        context = "\n\n".join([
            f"[文档 {i+1}] {chunk.content}"
            for i, chunk in enumerate(retrieved)
        ])
        
        # 3. 构建 Prompt
        prompt = f"""基于以下参考文档回答问题。如果文档中没有相关信息，请明确说明。

参考文档：
{context}

用户问题：{query}

请提供详细、准确的答案，并标注信息来源。"""
        
        # 4. 调用 LLM
        response = llm_client.chat.completions.create(
            model="gpt-4",
            messages=[
                {"role": "system", "content": "你是一个有帮助的助手，基于提供的文档回答问题。"},
                {"role": "user", "content": prompt}
            ],
            temperature=0.3
        )
        
        answer = response.choices[0].message.content
        
        # 5. 提取引用来源
        sources = [chunk.metadata.get("source", "未知") for chunk in retrieved]
        
        return {
            "query": query,
            "answer": answer,
            "sources": list(set(sources)),
            "retrieved_chunks": len(retrieved),
            "context_length": len(context)
        }

# 使用示例
if __name__ == "__main__":
    rag = RAGSystem()
    
    # 摄入文档
    rag.ingest_documents([
        "/data/docs/product_manual.pdf",
        "/data/docs/faq.docx"
    ])
    
    # 查询
    result = rag.generate("如何重置密码？", llm_client=openai_client)
    print(result["answer"])
```

### 16.2 RAG 评估框架

```python
# rag_evaluation.py
from datasets import Dataset
import pandas as pd

class RAGEvaluator:
    """RAG 系统评估器"""
    
    def __init__(self, rag_system):
        self.rag = rag_system
    
    def evaluate_retrieval(self, test_set: List[Dict]) -> Dict:
        """
        评估检索质量
        
        test_set: [{"query": str, "relevant_docs": List[str], "answer": str}]
        """
        metrics = {
            "recall@1": [],
            "recall@5": [],
            "recall@10": [],
            "mrr": [],
            "ndcg@5": []
        }
        
        for item in test_set:
            query = item["query"]
            relevant = set(item["relevant_docs"])
            
            retrieved = self.rag.retrieve(query, top_k=10)
            retrieved_ids = [r.metadata.get("doc_id") for r in retrieved]
            
            # Recall@K
            for k in [1, 5, 10]:
                hits = len(set(retrieved_ids[:k]) & relevant)
                metrics[f"recall@{k}"].append(hits / len(relevant))
            
            # MRR
            rr = 0
            for i, doc_id in enumerate(retrieved_ids):
                if doc_id in relevant:
                    rr = 1 / (i + 1)
                    break
            metrics["mrr"].append(rr)
            
            # NDCG
            dcg = sum(
                (1 / np.log2(i + 2)) 
                for i, doc_id in enumerate(retrieved_ids[:5])
                if doc_id in relevant
            )
            ideal_hits = min(len(relevant), 5)
            idcg = sum(1 / np.log2(i + 2) for i in range(ideal_hits))
            metrics["ndcg@5"].append(dcg / idcg if idcg > 0 else 0)
        
        return {k: np.mean(v) for k, v in metrics.items()}
    
    def evaluate_generation(self, test_set: List[Dict]) -> Dict:
        """
        评估生成质量（使用 RAGAS 指标）
        """
        from ragas.metrics import (
            answer_relevancy,
            faithfulness,
            context_recall,
            context_precision
        )
        from ragas import evaluate
        
        results = []
        for item in test_set:
            query = item["query"]
            ground_truth = item["answer"]
            
            result = self.rag.generate(query, llm_client=openai_client)
            
            results.append({
                "question": query,
                "answer": result["answer"],
                "contexts": [r.content for r in self.rag.retrieve(query)],
                "ground_truth": ground_truth
            })
        
        dataset = Dataset.from_pandas(pd.DataFrame(results))
        
        scores = evaluate(
            dataset,
            metrics=[
                answer_relevancy,
                faithfulness,
                context_recall,
                context_precision
            ]
        )
        
        return scores
```

## 第17章 Agent 系统完整实现

### 17.1 ReAct Agent 完整代码

```python
# react_agent.py
import json
import re
from typing import List, Dict, Callable, Optional
from dataclasses import dataclass, field
from enum import Enum

class ActionType(Enum):
    THOUGHT = "thought"
    ACTION = "action"
    OBSERVATION = "observation"
    FINAL = "final_answer"

@dataclass
class Step:
    thought: str
    action: Optional[str] = None
    action_input: Optional[str] = None
    observation: Optional[str] = None

class Tool:
    """工具基类"""
    
    def __init__(self, name: str, description: str, func: Callable):
        self.name = name
        self.description = description
        self.func = func
    
    def execute(self, **kwargs) -> str:
        try:
            result = self.func(**kwargs)
            return str(result)
        except Exception as e:
            return f"Error: {str(e)}"

class ReActAgent:
    """
    ReAct Agent 实现
    
    ReAct = Reasoning + Acting
    论文: "ReAct: Synergizing Reasoning and Acting in Language Models"
    """
    
    def __init__(self, llm_client, tools: List[Tool], max_steps=10):
        self.llm = llm_client
        self.tools = {tool.name: tool for tool in tools}
        self.max_steps = max_steps
        self.memory: List[Step] = []
    
    def _build_prompt(self, task: str) -> str:
        """构建 ReAct 格式的 Prompt"""
        
        tool_descriptions = "\n".join([
            f"{name}: {tool.description}"
            for name, tool in self.tools.items()
        ])
        
        history = ""
        for step in self.memory:
            history += f"Thought: {step.thought}\n"
            if step.action:
                history += f"Action: {step.action}[{step.action_input}]\n"
            if step.observation:
                history += f"Observation: {step.observation}\n"
        
        prompt = f"""解决以下任务。你可以使用以下工具：

{tool_descriptions}

请按以下格式思考：
Thought: [你的思考过程]
Action: [工具名][参数]
Observation: [工具返回结果]
...（重复 Thought/Action/Observation）
Thought: [最终结论]
Final Answer: [最终答案]

任务：{task}

{history}
Thought:"""
        
        return prompt
    
    def _parse_response(self, response: str) -> Dict:
        """解析 LLM 响应"""
        
        # 提取 Thought
        thought_match = re.search(r'Thought:\s*(.+?)(?=Action:|Final Answer:|$)', 
                                  response, re.DOTALL)
        thought = thought_match.group(1).strip() if thought_match else ""
        
        # 检查是否是最终答案
        final_match = re.search(r'Final Answer:\s*(.+)', response, re.DOTALL)
        if final_match:
            return {
                "type": ActionType.FINAL,
                "thought": thought,
                "answer": final_match.group(1).strip()
            }
        
        # 提取 Action
        action_match = re.search(r'Action:\s*(\w+)\[(.*?)\]', response, re.DOTALL)
        if action_match:
            return {
                "type": ActionType.ACTION,
                "thought": thought,
                "action": action_match.group(1).strip(),
                "action_input": action_match.group(2).strip()
            }
        
        return {
            "type": ActionType.THOUGHT,
            "thought": thought
        }
    
    def run(self, task: str) -> str:
        """运行 Agent"""
        
        for step in range(self.max_steps):
            # 构建 Prompt
            prompt = self._build_prompt(task)
            
            # 调用 LLM
            response = self.llm.chat.completions.create(
                model="gpt-4",
                messages=[{"role": "user", "content": prompt}],
                temperature=0.1,
                stop=["Observation:"]
            ).choices[0].message.content
            
            # 解析响应
            parsed = self._parse_response(response)
            
            if parsed["type"] == ActionType.FINAL:
                self.memory.append(Step(
                    thought=parsed["thought"]
                ))
                return parsed["answer"]
            
            if parsed["type"] == ActionType.ACTION:
                action_name = parsed["action"]
                action_input = parsed["action_input"]
                
                # 执行工具
                if action_name in self.tools:
                    try:
                        # 解析参数
                        params = json.loads(action_input) if action_input else {}
                        observation = self.tools[action_name].execute(**params)
                    except json.JSONDecodeError:
                        observation = self.tools[action_name].execute(query=action_input)
                else:
                    observation = f"Error: Tool '{action_name}' not found"
                
                # 记录步骤
                self.memory.append(Step(
                    thought=parsed["thought"],
                    action=action_name,
                    action_input=action_input,
                    observation=observation
                ))
            else:
                self.memory.append(Step(
                    thought=parsed["thought"]
                ))
        
        return "达到最大步数限制，未能完成任务。"

# 工具定义示例
def search_web(query: str) -> str:
    """模拟网络搜索"""
    # 实际实现中调用搜索引擎 API
    return f"搜索结果：关于 '{query}' 的信息..."

def calculate(expression: str) -> float:
    """计算表达式"""
    return eval(expression)

def read_file(path: str) -> str:
    """读取文件"""
    with open(path, 'r') as f:
        return f.read()

def execute_python(code: str) -> str:
    """执行 Python 代码（安全沙箱中）"""
    import subprocess
    result = subprocess.run(
        ['python', '-c', code],
        capture_output=True,
        text=True,
        timeout=5
    )
    return result.stdout or result.stderr

# 使用示例
tools = [
    Tool("search", "搜索网络信息", search_web),
    Tool("calculate", "计算数学表达式", calculate),
    Tool("read_file", "读取文件内容", read_file),
    Tool("python", "执行Python代码", execute_python)
]

agent = ReActAgent(llm_client=openai_client, tools=tools)
result = agent.run("2024年阿里巴巴的营收是多少？")
print(result)
```

### 17.2 Multi-Agent 系统

```python
# multi_agent.py
from typing import List, Callable
import threading
import queue

class AgentRole:
    """Agent 角色定义"""
    
    def __init__(self, name: str, system_prompt: str, skills: List[str]):
        self.name = name
        self.system_prompt = system_prompt
        self.skills = skills

class MultiAgentSystem:
    """
    多 Agent 协作系统
    
    包含：
    - Planner：任务规划
    - Executor：执行具体任务
    - Critic：审核和反馈
    """
    
    def __init__(self, llm_client):
        self.llm = llm_client
        self.agents = {}
        self.message_queue = queue.Queue()
    
    def register_agent(self, role: AgentRole, agent_instance):
        self.agents[role.name] = {
            "role": role,
            "instance": agent_instance
        }
    
    def plan(self, task: str) -> List[Dict]:
        """规划任务分解"""
        
        prompt = f"""将以下复杂任务分解为子任务列表。
每个子任务应包含：
- 任务描述
- 负责角色（planner/executor/researcher/coder）
- 依赖的前置任务

任务：{task}

请按 JSON 格式输出子任务列表："""
        
        response = self.llm.chat.completions.create(
            model="gpt-4",
            messages=[{"role": "user", "content": prompt}],
            response_format={"type": "json_object"}
        )
        
        plan = json.loads(response.choices[0].message.content)
        return plan.get("tasks", [])
    
    def execute_parallel(self, tasks: List[Dict]) -> Dict:
        """并行执行独立任务"""
        results = {}
        threads = []
        
        def run_task(task):
            role = task["role"]
            agent = self.agents.get(role, {}).get("instance")
            if agent:
                result = agent.run(task["description"])
                results[task["id"]] = result
        
        for task in tasks:
            if not task.get("dependencies"):
                t = threading.Thread(target=run_task, args=(task,))
                threads.append(t)
                t.start()
        
        for t in threads:
            t.join()
        
        return results
    
    def collaborate(self, task: str, max_rounds=3) -> str:
        """
        多 Agent 协作解决问题
        
        流程：
        1. Planner 分解任务
        2. Executor 执行子任务
        3. Critic 审核结果
        4. 如有问题，反馈给 Planner 重新规划
        """
        
        for round_num in range(max_rounds):
            # 1. 规划
            plan = self.plan(task)
            
            # 2. 执行
            results = self.execute_parallel(plan)
            
            # 3. 审核
            review_prompt = f"""审核以下任务执行结果：

原始任务：{task}
执行结果：{json.dumps(results, indent=2)}

请判断：
1. 结果是否完整、正确？
2. 是否需要补充或修正？
3. 如果通过，请总结最终答案。

请按 JSON 格式输出：
{{"passed": true/false, "feedback": "...", "final_answer": "..."}}"""
            
            review = self.llm.chat.completions.create(
                model="gpt-4",
                messages=[{"role": "user", "content": review_prompt}],
                response_format={"type": "json_object"}
            )
            
            review_result = json.loads(review.choices[0].message.content)
            
            if review_result.get("passed"):
                return review_result.get("final_answer", "")
            
            # 未通过，将反馈加入任务描述，重新规划
            task += f"\n\n上一轮反馈：{review_result.get('feedback')}"
        
        return "达到最大轮数限制。"
```

## 第18章 模型微调完整流程

### 18.1 数据准备完整流程

```python
# data_preparation.py
import json
import random
from typing import List, Dict
import jieba
from transformers import AutoTokenizer

class DataPreparer:
    """微调数据准备器"""
    
    def __init__(self, tokenizer_name="Qwen/Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct"):
        self.tokenizer = AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained(tokenizer_name)
    
    def load_raw_data(self, file_paths: List[str]) -> List[Dict]:
        """加载原始数据"""
        data = []
        for path in file_paths:
            with open(path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                if path.endswith('.jsonl'):
                    for line in f:
                        data.append(json.loads(line))
                elif path.endswith('.json'):
                    data.extend(json.load(f))
        return data
    
    def clean_text(self, text: str) -> str:
        """文本清洗"""
        # 去除多余空白
        text = ' '.join(text.split())
        # 去除特殊字符
        text = text.replace('\x00', '')
        # 统一标点
        text = text.replace('，', ',').replace('。', '.')
        return text
    
    def deduplicate(self, data: List[Dict], key='instruction') -> List[Dict]:
        """去重"""
        seen = set()
        unique = []
        for item in data:
            text = item.get(key, '')
            # 使用 SimHash 或 MinHash 进行模糊去重
            # 这里简化使用精确匹配
            if text not in seen:
                seen.add(text)
                unique.append(item)
        return unique
    
    def format_alpaca(self, instruction: str, input_text: str, output: str) -> str:
        """格式化为 Alpaca 格式"""
        if input_text:
            prompt = f"""Below is an instruction that describes a task, paired with an input that provides further context. Write a response that appropriately completes the request.

### Instruction:
{instruction}

### Input:
{input_text}

### Response:
"""
        else:
            prompt = f"""Below is an instruction that describes a task. Write a response that appropriately completes the request.

### Instruction:
{instruction}

### Response:
"""
        
        return prompt + output
    
    def format_sharegpt(self, conversations: List[Dict]) -> str:
        """格式化为 ShareGPT 格式"""
        formatted = ""
        for turn in conversations:
            role = turn["from"]
            content = turn["value"]
            if role == "human":
                formatted += f"<|im_start|>user\n{content}<|im_end|>\n"
            elif role == "gpt":
                formatted += f"<|im_start|>assistant\n{content}<|im_end|>\n"
        return formatted
    
    def create_training_examples(self, data: List[Dict], format_type="alpaca") -> List[Dict]:
        """创建训练样本"""
        examples = []
        
        for item in data:
            if format_type == "alpaca":
                text = self.format_alpaca(
                    item["instruction"],
                    item.get("input", ""),
                    item["output"]
                )
            elif format_type == "sharegpt":
                text = self.format_sharegpt(item["conversations"])
            else:
                text = item["text"]
            
            # Tokenize
            tokens = self.tokenizer(text, truncation=True, max_length=2048)
            
            examples.append({
                "text": text,
                "input_ids": tokens["input_ids"],
                "attention_mask": tokens["attention_mask"]
            })
        
        return examples
    
    def split_dataset(self, data: List[Dict], train_ratio=0.8, val_ratio=0.1):
        """划分数据集"""
        random.shuffle(data)
        
        n = len(data)
        train_end = int(n * train_ratio)
        val_end = int(n * (train_ratio + val_ratio))
        
        return {
            "train": data[:train_end],
            "validation": data[train_end:val_end],
            "test": data[val_end:]
        }
    
    def prepare(self, file_paths: List[str], output_dir: str, format_type="alpaca"):
        """完整数据准备流程"""
        # 1. 加载
        raw_data = self.load_raw_data(file_paths)
        print(f"Loaded {len(raw_data)} raw examples")
        
        # 2. 清洗
        cleaned = [{k: self.clean_text(v) if isinstance(v, str) else v 
                   for k, v in item.items()} 
                  for item in raw_data]
        
        # 3. 去重
        deduped = self.deduplicate(cleaned)
        print(f"After dedup: {len(deduped)} examples")
        
        # 4. 格式化
        examples = self.create_training_examples(deduped, format_type)
        
        # 5. 划分
        splits = self.split_dataset(examples)
        
        # 6. 保存
        for split_name, split_data in splits.items():
            output_path = f"{output_dir}/{split_name}.jsonl"
            with open(output_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                for item in split_data:
                    f.write(json.dumps(item, ensure_ascii=False) + '\n')
            print(f"Saved {len(split_data)} examples to {output_path}")
        
        return splits
```

### 18.2 LoRA 微调完整代码

```python
# lora_training.py
import torch
from torch.utils.data import Dataset, DataLoader
from transformers import (
    AutoModelForCausalLM,
    AutoTokenizer,
    TrainingArguments,
    Trainer,
    DataCollatorForLanguageModeling
)
from peft import (
    LoraConfig,
    get_peft_model,
    prepare_model_for_kbit_training,
    TaskType
)
from datasets import load_dataset
import wandb

class InstructionDataset(Dataset):
    """指令微调数据集"""
    
    def __init__(self, data_path, tokenizer, max_length=2048):
        self.tokenizer = tokenizer
        self.max_length = max_length
        
        with open(data_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
            self.data = [json.loads(line) for line in f]
    
    def __len__(self):
        return len(self.data)
    
    def __getitem__(self, idx):
        item = self.data[idx]
        text = item["text"]
        
        encoding = self.tokenizer(
            text,
            truncation=True,
            max_length=self.max_length,
            padding="max_length",
            return_tensors="pt"
        )
        
        return {
            "input_ids": encoding["input_ids"].flatten(),
            "attention_mask": encoding["attention_mask"].flatten(),
            "labels": encoding["input_ids"].flatten()
        }

def setup_lora_model(model_name, r=64, lora_alpha=128, target_modules=None):
    """设置 LoRA 模型"""
    
    # 加载基础模型
    model = AutoModelForCausalLM.from_pretrained(
        model_name,
        torch_dtype=torch.bfloat16,
        device_map="auto",
        trust_remote_code=True
    )
    
    # 准备模型（梯度检查点等）
    model = prepare_model_for_kbit_training(model)
    
    # 默认目标模块
    if target_modules is None:
        target_modules = [
            "q_proj", "k_proj", "v_proj", "o_proj",
            "gate_proj", "up_proj", "down_proj"
        ]
    
    # LoRA 配置
    lora_config = LoraConfig(
        r=r,
        lora_alpha=lora_alpha,
        target_modules=target_modules,
        lora_dropout=0.05,
        bias="none",
        task_type=TaskType.CAUSAL_LM,
        # 使用 DoRA（权重分解低秩适应）
        use_dora=True,
    )
    
    # 应用 LoRA
    model = get_peft_model(model, lora_config)
    model.print_trainable_parameters()
    
    return model

def train(
    model_name="Qwen/Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct",
    data_path="./data/train.jsonl",
    output_dir="./outputs",
    num_epochs=3,
    batch_size=4,
    learning_rate=2e-4,
    r=64,
    lora_alpha=128
):
    """训练流程"""
    
    # 1. 初始化 wandb（可选）
    wandb.init(project="llm-finetune", name=f"{model_name.split('/')[-1]}-lora")
    
    # 2. 加载 tokenizer
    tokenizer = AutoTokenizer.from_pretrained(model_name, trust_remote_code=True)
    tokenizer.pad_token = tokenizer.eos_token
    
    # 3. 设置 LoRA 模型
    model = setup_lora_model(model_name, r=r, lora_alpha=lora_alpha)
    
    # 4. 加载数据集
    train_dataset = InstructionDataset(data_path, tokenizer)
    
    # 5. 数据整理器
    data_collator = DataCollatorForLanguageModeling(
        tokenizer=tokenizer,
        mlm=False
    )
    
    # 6. 训练参数
    training_args = TrainingArguments(
        output_dir=output_dir,
        num_train_epochs=num_epochs,
        per_device_train_batch_size=batch_size,
        gradient_accumulation_steps=4,
        learning_rate=learning_rate,
        weight_decay=0.01,
        warmup_ratio=0.03,
        lr_scheduler_type="cosine",
        logging_steps=10,
        save_steps=500,
        save_total_limit=3,
        bf16=True,
        tf32=True,
        report_to="wandb",
        remove_unused_columns=False,
        gradient_checkpointing=True,  # 节省显存
    )
    
    # 7. 创建 Trainer
    trainer = Trainer(
        model=model,
        args=training_args,
        train_dataset=train_dataset,
        data_collator=data_collator,
    )
    
    # 8. 训练
    trainer.train()
    
    # 9. 保存模型
    model.save_pretrained(f"{output_dir}/final")
    tokenizer.save_pretrained(f"{output_dir}/final")
    
    # 10. 合并权重（可选）
    merged_model = model.merge_and_unload()
    merged_model.save_pretrained(f"{output_dir}/merged")
    
    wandb.finish()
    
    return model

# QLoRA 训练（4-bit 量化，更低显存）
def train_qlora(
    model_name="Qwen/Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct",
    data_path="./data/train.jsonl",
    output_dir="./outputs-qlora",
    **kwargs
):
    """QLoRA 训练（适合消费级显卡）"""
    
    from transformers import BitsAndBytesConfig
    
    # 4-bit 量化配置
    bnb_config = BitsAndBytesConfig(
        load_in_4bit=True,
        bnb_4bit_quant_type="nf4",  # Normal Float 4
        bnb_4bit_compute_dtype=torch.bfloat16,
        bnb_4bit_use_double_quant=True,  # 嵌套量化
    )
    
    # 加载量化模型
    model = AutoModelForCausalLM.from_pretrained(
        model_name,
        quantization_config=bnb_config,
        device_map="auto",
        trust_remote_code=True
    )
    
    # 准备用于训练
    model = prepare_model_for_kbit_training(model)
    
    # 应用 LoRA
    lora_config = LoraConfig(
        r=64,
        lora_alpha=16,
        target_modules=["q_proj", "k_proj", "v_proj", "o_proj"],
        lora_dropout=0.1,
        bias="none",
        task_type=TaskType.CAUSAL_LM,
    )
    
    model = get_peft_model(model, lora_config)
    
    # ... 后续训练流程与 LoRA 相同
    
    return model
```

## 第19章 行业落地案例集

### 19.1 金融行业：智能投研助手

#### 业务场景

为券商研究所搭建智能投研助手，能够：
- 阅读和理解财报、研报
- 回答行业和公司相关问题
- 生成投资建议摘要

#### 技术方案

```
架构设计：

数据源层
├── 财报数据库（Wind/同花顺）
├── 研报 PDF（内部 + 外部）
├── 新闻资讯（财经媒体）
└── 公告信息（交易所）

处理层
├── 文档解析（表格/图表/文本）
├── 实体识别（公司/人物/指标）
├── 关系抽取（产业链/股权）
└── 向量化存储

RAG 层
├── 混合检索（向量 + 关键词 + 时间筛选）
├── 重排序（金融专业模型）
└── 引用溯源

生成层
├── 70B 金融微调模型
├── 数字精确性校验
└── 合规审查过滤
```

**关键挑战与解决：**

| 挑战 | 解决方案 |
|------|----------|
| 表格数据理解 | 专用表格解析器 + 结构化表示 |
| 数字精确性 | RAG 检索原始数据 + LLM 生成时标注来源 |
| 合规风险 | 输出前经合规规则引擎审核 |
| 实时性 | 新闻数据 5 分钟增量更新到向量库 |

**效果数据：**
- 研报阅读效率提升 5 倍
- 投资问答准确率 92%
- 分析师满意度 4.5/5

### 19.2 医疗行业：辅助诊断系统

#### 业务场景

三甲医院搭建病历分析和辅助诊断系统：
- 理解患者主诉和病史
- 推荐可能的诊断方向
- 生成病历摘要

#### 技术方案

```
数据层
├── 电子病历（结构化 + 非结构化）
├── 医学文献（PubMed/知网）
├── 临床指南（NCCN/中华医学会）
└── 药品说明书

RAG 层
├── 医学术语标准化（ICD-10/SNOMED）
├── 多模态检索（文本 + 影像报告）
└── 证据等级标注

生成层
├── 医学微调模型（基于 PubMed 文献）
├── 不确定性表达（"可能"/"建议进一步检查"）
└── 禁忌症提醒
```

**关键挑战：**
- 隐私保护：数据不出院，本地部署
- 责任界定：明确标注"仅供参考，不作为诊断依据"
- 多模态：整合检验报告、影像描述

### 19.3 电商行业：智能导购

#### 业务场景

电商平台智能导购系统：
- 理解用户模糊需求（"适合夏天穿的舒服鞋子"）
- 推荐商品并解释原因
- 处理售后咨询

#### 技术方案

```
知识库
├── 商品信息（标题/描述/参数）
├── 用户评价（情感分析后入库）
├── 穿搭知识（场景/季节/风格）
└── 售后政策

RAG 增强
├── 实时库存和价格
├── 用户画像（历史购买/浏览）
└── 促销信息

Agent 能力
├── 多轮对话澄清需求
├── 商品对比（参数/价格/评价）
└── 下单引导（加入购物车/立即购买）
```

**效果数据：**
- 转化率提升 15%
- 客服人力节省 40%
- 用户满意度 4.3/5

### 19.4 法律行业：合同审查

#### 业务场景

律所和公司法务部门使用 AI 辅助合同审查：
- 识别风险条款
- 对比不同版本差异
- 生成审查意见

#### 技术方案

```
知识库
├── 法律法规（民法典/合同法/劳动法）
├── 判例数据库
├── 标准合同模板
└── 公司内部审批规则

RAG 增强
├── 相似合同检索
├── 风险条款库匹配
└── 当事人背景查询

生成层
├── 法律微调模型
├── 条款风险等级标注（高/中/低）
└── 修改建议生成
```

### 19.5 教育行业：智能答疑

#### 业务场景

在线教育平台智能答疑系统：
- 回答学科问题（数学/物理/化学）
- 逐步引导解题思路
- 批改作业并给出反馈

#### 技术方案

```
知识库
├── 教材内容（各版本）
├── 题库（题目 + 解析）
├── 知识点图谱
└── 常见错误分析

Agent 能力
├── 题目理解（识别已知/所求）
├── 解题规划（选择公式/方法）
├── 逐步推导（展示中间步骤）
└── 错误诊断（分析学生错因）

特殊处理
├── 数学公式渲染（LaTeX）
├── 图形题理解（几何/函数图像）
└── 代码题执行（Python 沙箱）
```

## 第20章 ROI 计算与成本控制

### 20.1 详细成本模型

```python
class LLMCostModel:
    """LLM 服务成本模型"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.gpu_costs = {
            "RTX_4090": {"hourly": 1.5, "power_kw": 0.45},
            "A100_40G": {"hourly": 2.0, "power_kw": 0.25},
            "A100_80G": {"hourly": 3.0, "power_kw": 0.30},
            "H100": {"hourly": 5.0, "power_kw": 0.70},
            "L40S": {"hourly": 2.5, "power_kw": 0.35},
        }
        self.electricity_cost_per_kwh = 0.8  # 元
    
    def calculate(self, gpu_type, num_gpus, utilization, daily_hours=24):
        """
        计算月度成本
        
        gpu_type: GPU 型号
        num_gpus: GPU 数量
        utilization: 平均利用率（0-1）
        daily_hours: 每日运行小时数
        """
        gpu_info = self.gpu_costs[gpu_type]
        
        # 计算成本
        days_per_month = 30
        
        # 1. GPU 租赁成本
        gpu_cost = gpu_info["hourly"] * num_gpus * daily_hours * days_per_month
        
        # 2. 电力成本
        power_cost = (
            gpu_info["power_kw"] * num_gpus * 
            utilization * daily_hours * days_per_month * 
            self.electricity_cost_per_kwh
        )
        
        # 3. 机房/网络/人力（估算）
        overhead = gpu_cost * 0.3  # 30%  overhead
        
        total = gpu_cost + power_cost + overhead
        
        # 计算单 token 成本
        # 假设：H100 在 80% 利用率下，吞吐 80 tokens/s
        if gpu_type == "H100":
            tokens_per_second = 80 * utilization
        elif gpu_type == "A100_80G":
            tokens_per_second = 40 * utilization
        else:
            tokens_per_second = 30 * utilization
        
        total_tokens = tokens_per_second * num_gpus * daily_hours * 3600 * days_per_month
        cost_per_million = (total / total_tokens) * 1_000_000
        
        return {
            "gpu_cost": gpu_cost,
            "power_cost": power_cost,
            "overhead": overhead,
            "total_monthly": total,
            "cost_per_million_tokens": cost_per_million,
            "total_tokens_per_month": total_tokens
        }
    
    def compare_deployments(self, scenarios):
        """对比不同部署方案"""
        results = []
        for name, config in scenarios.items():
            cost = self.calculate(**config)
            results.append({
                "name": name,
                **cost,
                **config
            })
        
        return pd.DataFrame(results)

# 使用示例
model = LLMCostModel()

scenarios = {
    "方案A_消费级": {
        "gpu_type": "RTX_4090",
        "num_gpus": 8,
        "utilization": 0.8,
        "daily_hours": 24
    },
    "方案B_云A100": {
        "gpu_type": "A100_80G",
        "num_gpus": 4,
        "utilization": 0.85,
        "daily_hours": 24
    },
    "方案C_云H100": {
        "gpu_type": "H100",
        "num_gpus": 2,
        "utilization": 0.9,
        "daily_hours": 24
    }
}

comparison = model.compare_deployments(scenarios)
print(comparison[["name", "total_monthly", "cost_per_million_tokens"]])
```

### 20.2 ROI 计算模板

```python
def calculate_roi(
    # 投入
    infrastructure_cost_monthly,
    development_cost_one_time,
    maintenance_cost_monthly,
    
    # 产出
    labor_hours_saved_monthly,
    labor_cost_per_hour,
    new_revenue_monthly,
    customer_satisfaction_improvement,  # 0-1
    
    # 时间范围
    months=12
):
    """计算 ROI"""
    
    # 总投入
    total_investment = (
        development_cost_one_time +
        (infrastructure_cost_monthly + maintenance_cost_monthly) * months
    )
    
    # 总收益
    labor_savings = labor_hours_saved_monthly * labor_cost_per_hour * months
    revenue_increase = new_revenue_monthly * months
    
    # 满意度提升带来的间接收益（估算）
    satisfaction_value = new_revenue_monthly * customer_satisfaction_improvement * months * 0.1
    
    total_benefit = labor_savings + revenue_increase + satisfaction_value
    
    # ROI
    roi = (total_benefit - total_investment) / total_investment * 100
    
    # 回本周期
    monthly_net = (labor_hours_saved_monthly * labor_cost_per_hour + 
                   new_revenue_monthly - infrastructure_cost_monthly - maintenance_cost_monthly)
    payback_months = development_cost_one_time / monthly_net if monthly_net > 0 else float('inf')
    
    return {
        "total_investment": total_investment,
        "total_benefit": total_benefit,
        "net_profit": total_benefit - total_investment,
        "roi_percent": roi,
        "payback_months": payback_months,
        "monthly_net": monthly_net
    }

# 示例：智能客服系统 ROI
result = calculate_roi(
    infrastructure_cost_monthly=50000,  # 5万/月（GPU+运维）
    development_cost_one_time=200000,   # 20万（一次性开发）
    maintenance_cost_monthly=10000,     # 1万/月（维护）
    labor_hours_saved_monthly=2000,     # 节省2000人时/月
    labor_cost_per_hour=50,             # 50元/人时
    new_revenue_monthly=30000,          # 新增3万/月（转化率提升）
    customer_satisfaction_improvement=0.15,
    months=12
)

print(f"ROI: {result['roi_percent']:.1f}%")
print(f"回本周期: {result['payback_months']:.1f} 个月")
```
